Central Political Conference 80

▲ Two Hundred and Twenty-Third Meeting

The Central Political Conference held its 223rd meeting at 8:00 AM today (16th). The attending members were Hu Hanmin, Gu Yingfen, Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Chonghui, Sun Ke, Song Ziwen, Shao Lizi, Ye Chucang, and Wu Jingheng. The attending members were Shao Yuan

Page 8

Chong, Li Fuyi, Wang Zhengting, Li Wenlong, Kong Xiangxi, and Liu Luyin. The chairman was Chiang Kai-shek. The discussion items were as follows: (1) Member and President of the Judicial Yuan Wang Chonghui proposed that, according to the National Government's order on June 27th of the Republic of China, if any national citizen intends to insult the portrait of the Premier of the Chinese Kuomintang, publicly damages, removes, or insults it, they should be punished in accordance with Article 167 of the Criminal Law, the same as those who damage, remove, or insult the national flag and national emblem of the Republic of China. If there is such behavior after the order was issued on June 27th of the Republic of China, they should be punished according to the law. However, if there is such behavior before the order was issued, according to the principle stated in Article 1 of the Criminal Law, since there was no law imposing criminal punishment at the time of the behavior, it should not be considered a crime. The question is whether the behavior before the order was issued should not be considered a crime, or whether it should be retroactively pursued. Please make a decision. The resolution was not to pursue it retroactively. (2) The National Government Civil Service Department stated that the 71st State Council meeting resolved to specially appoint Liu Ruiheng as the Minister of Health. Since it concerns the appointment and removal of specially appointed officials, it should be forwarded to the Central Political Conference for retroactive approval to comply with the established regulations. The resolution was to grant retroactive approval.

The Second Day of the Capital Construction Conference 81

The Capital Construction Committee held a group proposal review committee on the morning of the 16th, followed immediately by the first general meeting. The proceedings are summarized as follows:

▲ Group Review Committee

At 8:00 AM, members of the first, second, and third groups gathered at the meeting place and began reviewing proposals. The attendance was enthusiastic, and results were achieved for all proposals. These were then submitted to the general meeting report. The meeting adjourned around 10:00 AM.

▲ First General Meeting

After the review committee adjourned, the original agenda called for a work report from the committee. All members attended, including Zhang Renjie, Sun Ke, Wang Chonghui, Zhu Peide, Wang Zhengting, Li Chugong, Chen Yu, Kong Xiangxi, Liu Ruiheng, Wei Daoming, Yang Zongjian, Dong Xiujia, Shen Yi, Qin Hua, Liu Jiwen, Shao Yuanchong, Yang Xiji, Ma Fuxiang, Tang Zhi, Lai Lian, Yuan Hui, Lu Rushan, Xu Chaotong, Wu Bizhi, Wang Nu, Chen Yi, Xia Guangyu, Jin Guobao, Schubart, Zhang Yiou, Zhang Zhijiang, Chen Rui, and Zhang Jianming, totaling 24 people. Thirteen observers were present. The meeting commenced at 10:30 AM, with Zhang Renjie as chairman. After formalities, Secretary-General Liu Jiwen reported that the attendance met the legal quorum and declared the meeting open. Secretary Hong Lanyou reported that, according to the agenda, a work report was still pending, but it had already been distributed to all members. To save time, it would not be presented orally, and the discussion would immediately commence on the reports from each group of the review committee. After Hong's report, each group member reported the review results as follows:

First Group Review Report: Reviewer Xu Xinwu reported the review results, stating that the committee reviewed the following cases: (1) Case 51 proposed by committee member Sun Ke and Case 5 proposed by advisor Schubart regarding the central political zone. The two cases differed slightly on the zone issue. Sun proposed locating the zone south of Zhongshan Road, while Schubart argued that it should not be confined to Zhongshan Road and that attention should be paid to preserving historical sites. The review committee's opinion was that it should not be limited to the business of Zhongshan Road, but should include the entire Ming Palace area and pay attention to the preservation of historical sites, in line with government orders. As the detailed arrangements could not be decided in a short time, it was proposed that they be submitted to the engineering group for further study. After the report, members expressed their opinions, and it was resolved to adopt the review committee's opinion and instruct the engineering group to formulate detailed measures. (2) Regarding the capital construction work allocation timetable, committee member Liu Jiwen proposed strictly defining the capital construction work schedule and setting a deadline for completion, while committee member Sun Ke proposed formulating procedures for the implementation of the city plan. The two cases were generally the same, but differed slightly in the details of the work. The review concluded that the principle of phased construction should be adopted, but the overall capital construction plan and fundraising had not yet been decided. It was proposed that, after the completion of the overall plan and the fundraising, the standing committee would formulate detailed measures. After the chairman put it to a vote, it was resolved to adopt the review report. (3) Cases 33, 34, 45, and 56. Except for Case 45, which was not discussed jointly, the remaining three cases concerned the location of the central station, the layout of railway lines within the capital, and Liu Jiwen's proposal to locate the central station in Xiaoying, while Sun Ke proposed locating the central station north of Houzaimen. Schubart proposed establishing a small station in addition to the central station, separating passenger and freight stations. The review committee believed that Schubart's railway line traversed the capital area and was related to road traffic, so it should encircle the area to avoid obstruction. At the same time, the review committee considered this matter to be of great importance and did not formulate specific measures. It was proposed that the Capital Construction Committee and the Ministry of Railways decide on the measures. After the chairman put it to a discussion, it was resolved to adopt the review committee's opinion. Case 45 was a proposal by committee member Kong to complete the Beijing-Xiangtan Railway. The review committee considered that this was beyond the authority of the committee and should be handled by the Ministry of Railways. Kong Xiangxi then stood up to explain the reasons, stating that it was greatly related to capital construction. The general meeting then resolved to request the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Railways to handle it as soon as possible.

Second Group Review Report: Committee member Kong Xiangxi reported on the capital construction funding and fundraising matters, submitting Case 37 on the implementation plan for capital construction bonds and Case 30 on the proposed methods for promoting capital construction bonds for a public resolution, which were merged with Case 28 on the proposed implementation plan for allocating capital construction funding among the provinces. The result was to issue 30 million in capital construction bonds according to Case 28, with the methods in Cases 37 and 30 as reference. After the chairman put it to a vote, it was resolved to adopt it. The group also reviewed Case 7, a proposal by He Jian on opinions regarding capital zoning and construction funding. The review committee considered that the construction of the capital should be funded by the government, but within the possible scope, the principle of attracting merchants to invest should be adopted. This case could be submitted to the standing committee for adoption. Case 44, proposed by Kong Xiangxi, stipulated that each province and city should be responsible for building capital routes and encouraged overseas Chinese to donate funds for construction. The review committee considered that this case could be merged with Case 27, proposed by Liu Jiwen, stating that the capital trunk roads should be built by each province, with the name of each province as the name of each road. The methods proposed in the original proposal were still appropriate and could be adopted as is. Case 36, proposed by Liu Jiwen, requested the allocation of funds for sewers to facilitate capital construction. The review committee considered that the main purpose of this case was still sound, but the stated amount of waste discharged per person per day in Nanjing, whether 200 gallons or 60 gallons, should be reviewed by the engineering group, and whether this cost was within the initial capital construction cost of 50 million should be discussed and decided by the standing committee. After the report, the secretariat submitted each case for discussion by the general meeting, which then passed each item. The meeting adjourned around 12:00 PM.

▲ Summary of Resolutions

The cases reviewed by the first group and resolved by the general meeting are as follows: (1) Sun Ke's proposal to define the scope of the central political zone and build it, and Liu Jiwen's introduction of advisor Schubart's proposal to prepare drawings of the layout of the central political zone for adoption, were discussed jointly. The resolution was that the scope of the central political zone should be relocated in accordance with the previous order of the National Government, and the principles proposed by Schubart were adopted. The detailed plan was submitted to the engineering group for joint research. (2) Liu Jiwen's proposal to determine the capital construction work schedule and completion deadline, and Sun Ke's proposal to formulate procedures for the implementation of the city plan, were discussed jointly. The resolution was that the principle of phased construction should be adopted, but many of the projects to be undertaken have not yet been decided, and the phased construction process is closely related to economic issues. After the completion of the overall plan, the standing committee should refer to the fundraising methods for economic issues and resolve them appropriately before determining detailed phased measures to suit the plans and economic conditions of the ministry. (3) Liu Jiwen's proposal to determine the location of the station in the city in advance in order to complete the road system, and Sun Ke's proposal to continue to follow the original plan of the Capital Design Office and locate the central station north of Houzaimen in the Ming Palace, and Liu Jiwen's introduction of advisor Schubart's proposal to prepare a capital railway system and station location plan for public resolution, were discussed jointly. The resolution was that the location of the central station and the layout of railway lines in the capital area would be submitted to the standing committee to be reviewed and approved by the Ministry of Railways. (4) Kong Xiangxi's proposal to advance the Beijing-Xiangtan Railway to promote the development of the capital was resolved to be adopted as is, and a request was sent to the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Railways to handle it. Second group: (1) He Jian's proposal regarding opinions on capital zoning and construction funding, submitted for public resolution, was resolved to be submitted to the standing committee for adoption. (2) Liu Jiwen's proposal to raise funds for sewers to facilitate capital construction was resolved to be adopted in principle, and technical issues were submitted to the standing committee for handling. (3) Kong Xiangxi's proposal to stipulate that each province and city should be responsible for building capital routes and to encourage overseas Chinese to donate funds for construction, and Liu Jiwen's proposal that the capital trunk roads should be built by each province, with the name of each province as the name of each road, were discussed jointly. The resolution was to adopt it in principle and submit it to the standing committee for proper handling. (4) Liu Jiwen's proposal to formulate an implementation plan for each province to share the capital construction funding, submitted for public resolution, and Kong Xiangxi's proposal for the capital construction bond implementation plan were discussed jointly. The resolution was to adopt it. (5) Liu Jiwen's proposal to formulate methods for promoting capital construction bonds, submitted for public resolution, was resolved to be submitted to the standing committee for reference.

▲ The Third Group Held a Meeting in the Afternoon

The third group was originally scheduled to meet in the morning, but it did not materialize due to circumstances. Therefore, the group did not report at the first general meeting. The group held a special meeting in the afternoon to discuss the proposals and decided to submit them to the general meeting for discussion tomorrow.

▲ Temporary Review Group Meeting Held in the Afternoon

The general meeting was originally scheduled to continue in the afternoon, but it was rescheduled for tomorrow morning due to the need to hold a temporary review group meeting in the afternoon. The temporary review group met at 3:00 PM, attended by committee members Wei Daoming, Liu Ruiheng, Liu Jiwen, Dong Xiujia, Shen Yi, Liu Luyin, Hong Lanyou, Chen Yu, and Ye Chucang. They reviewed Zhang Renjie's proposal to request the National Government to allocate funds to complete the capital street light installation within a specified period, Li Zonghuang's proposal that the construction of the capital should be based on the principles of simplicity, solemnity, and garden city, and that the capital plan should be completed within the shortest possible period, and that the land prices of private land requisitioned for Zhongshan Road should be repaid as soon as possible, and Liu Wendao's proposal on how to raise the huge capital construction funds.

The Preconditions of the Civil Code's Family and Inheritance Sections 82

▲ Hu Hanmin and Lin Sen requested the Central Political Committee to decide

The Civil Code Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan has successively completed the drafting of the General Principles, Obligations, and Property Rights sections, which were passed by the Yuan and promulgated by the National Government. It then began drafting the Family and Inheritance sections. However, these two sections are of great concern to the Kuomintang's party platform and local customs. If they are not carefully considered, their implementation will inevitably be inconsistent. Therefore, Yuan President Hu Hanmin and Lin Sen specifically submitted the points that should be decided first for these two laws to the Central Political Conference for decision. The Central Political Conference has handed them over to the Legal Group for review, which is currently underway. The original text of the points that Hu and Lin proposed should be decided first for these two sections is as follows:

"Regarding the proposal, all three sections of the Civil Code, the first section on General Principles, the second section on Obligations, and the third section on Property Rights, have been successively promulgated by the National Government. The fourth section on Family and the fifth section on Inheritance urgently need to be drafted to facilitate their application. However, these two sections on Family and Inheritance are of great concern to our party's platform and local customs. If they are not carefully considered, I am afraid there will be many inconsistencies. It is proposed that the committee first formulate principles and issue them to the Legislative Yuan to follow in drafting, to comply with the legislative procedures. The most controversial points in terms of legislative doctrine are submitted for preliminary decision, so that there is something to refer to when formulating principles. This is the proposal, please decide publicly. Proposers: Hu Hanmin, Lin Sen.

▲ Points to be decided first in Family Law: (1) How should relatives be classified and what should be their scope? According to the classification of relatives, in addition to husband and wife, our old law has traditionally divided them into three categories: clan relatives, maternal relatives, and wife's relatives. Relatives of the male lineage descended from the same ancestor are called clan relatives. Relatives connected by the female lineage are called maternal relatives. The relationship with the wife's natural relatives through marriage is called wife's relatives. However, foreign laws divide them into two categories: consanguineous relatives and affinal relatives. Relatives born of blood relationship are called consanguineous relatives. Relatives born of marital relationship are called affinal relatives. How should our Family Law be stipulated? This is the first point for preliminary decision. If blood and marriage are the criteria for classifying relatives, then the issue of surnames between husband and wife and children should also be resolved. How should our Family Law be stipulated? This is the second point for preliminary decision. Thinking about kinship from a natural point of view, the scope is extremely broad. If the number of generations is too distant, not only is it practically no different from non-relatives, but it is also unnecessary to recognize them as relatives in law. Therefore, the laws of various countries generally set certain limits to limit the scope of relatives. How should our Family Law be stipulated? This is the third point for preliminary decision. (To be continued)

The Recent Trend of the War Situation in Guangxi Province 83

▲ Observations on Zhang Guijun Abandoning Guangxi to Enter Hunan and Attack Fuyang River

Guangzhou Communication: The military situation in Guangxi has been quiet for the past month. Both sides have been making deployments and movements. Until recently, the tense situation in the Central Plains has also affected the war situation in the Southwest. Therefore, in recent days, the war situation in Guangxi Province has undergone new changes again. Currently, Zhang Guijun's movements are quite erratic. The Sixth and Eighth Armies can only proceed step by step and cannot penetrate deep into the interior of Guangxi Province. After Zhang's army retreated from Qinlian on the southern route of Guangdong Province to Yongchun and Hengxian along the Guangxi border, it gradually moved north with Li Zongren's and Tang Shengming's troops. It now seems to have concentrated in Guixian. At the same time, Huang Shaoxiong's troops in Guiping have also reportedly transferred a portion of their troops, appearing to bypass and attack along the Fuyang River. Therefore, Zhu Shaoliang's Sixth Army on the Dahe side cannot penetrate deep into Pingnan and Guiping. Currently, Mao Bingwen, Tan Daoyuan, and Xu Kexiang's units of the Sixth Army are concentrated between Tengxian and Mengjiang, with Zhu Weizhen and Zhou Xinming's newly formed Guangxi soldiers as vanguards and guides. As of the 6th of this month, the Sixth Route Army's vanguard only reached Dawuwei, 75 li above Mengjiang. This place is still 65 li away from Pingnan. On the surface, it appears that Zhu's Sixth Route Army is containing the enemy in Pingnan and Guiping, while the various divisions under Chen Jitang's First Route Army are attacking Guixian below Guiping, which is easier. Currently, Jiang Guangnai's division of the Eighth Route Army is pressing towards Guixian, and Li Deying's regiment of Lu Huan'yan's division advanced from Xingye to Qiaowei on the 6th (Qiaowei is 60 li from Guixian), serving as the vanguard. Cai Tingkai's division also continued to advance to Shanxinwei, the border between Xingye and Guixian. On the 8th, parts of Jiang and Cai's divisions had advanced to Putang and dispatched Qu Shounian's brigade of Cai's division to Xiawan to monitor the south bank of Guiping. The First Independent Regiment of the General Headquarters, led by Fan Dexing, joined the Pingnan line with the Sixth Route Army, and Li Yang's police division followed and advanced towards Xingye. As for Yu Hanmou and Xiang Hanping's divisions, they concentrated in Luwu in the Qinshu area of Guangdong Province to guard Yongchun on the Guangxi border. It is reported that Li Deying's regiment of Lu's vanguard in Xingye completed the river crossing on the 7th and pressed towards Sanpingluobowan, Guixian. However, the enemy in Guixian is still relying on the terrain to hold firm, and there has not been much contact between the two sides. In recent days, Zhang Guijun has not taken any active actions in Guixian and Guiping. According to a certain source yesterday, a part of Zhang Guijun's army in Guiping and Guixian retreated to Wuxuan on the 7th. Therefore, there are two speculations about Zhang Guijun's actions. One says that Zhang Guijun has been facing difficulties in logistics and has repeatedly failed to attack Guangdong. If this stalemate continues, it may lead to annihilation. Taking advantage of the current situation in the Central Plains, they may simply unite and lead their troops through southern Hunan to the Yangtze River to respond to Yan and Feng in order to find a way out. They will abandon the Guangxi territory and move their troops to Quanzhou. The retreat from Guiping in recent days may be to implement their plan to enter Hunan. Another says that Zhang Guijun's military operations have always been secretive. This time, they are shortening the defense line step by step, and the retreat from Guiping seems to be luring the Sixth and Eighth Routes of Dahe to penetrate deep into Guiping and Guixian, and then send heavy troops to attack Fuyang River and attack Wuzhou, cutting off the rear of the Sixth and Eighth Routes. According to recent investigations, only Huang Shaoxiong, Li Zongren, and Zhang Fakui's troops are in the Guiping and Guixian area. Bai Chongxi's whereabouts are unknown. It is suspected that Bai's troops are actually out of Zhaoping, peeping at Majiang and Cangwu. Therefore, in the Guixian area, the Eighth Route Army is only led by the Chief of Staff of the Eighth Army, who is based in Yulin, while the Commander-in-Chief Chen Jitang is still sitting in Wuzhou. The above two theories both have considerable merit, and they are recorded here to await proof of the facts. (April 11)

Guangdong-Northern Jiang Communist Bandits Have Retreated to the Jiangxi Border 84

▲ Guangdong and Jiangxi Armies Are Currently Sending Troops to Encircle and Suppress the Jiangxi Border

Guangzhou Communication: After the Communist bandits Zhu and Peng sneaked into Nanxiong, Shixing, and Renhua counties on the Jiangxi border, they initially planned to attack Shaocheng from Shixing. Later, after learning that the provincial army's six regiments had deployed in Jilongwei and Zhoutian, they took the initiative to withdraw from Shixing and Nanxiong on the morning of the 8th. According to a source, the Communist bandits Zhu and Peng occupied Xiongshi for a total of seven days. There were no less than five or six thousand Communist bandits, led by Zhu De and Peng Dehuai. On the 1st of this month, they occupied Nanxiong from Dagen, on the 2nd they arrived in Gushi, on the 3rd they occupied Mashi, and on the 4th they entered Shixing. Wherever they went, plainclothes Communist bandits rose up to provide internal support, so the local militia and police were caught off guard. When the Communist bandits were in Xiong, they extorted no less than sixty to seventy thousand yuan from merchants and confiscated about twenty to thirty thousand yuan in public funds. At 5 p.m. on the 1st, the defending army retreated due to weakness. At 7 p.m., more than 100 Communist bandits first entered Xiong City. At 9 a.m. on the 2nd, a large number of Communist bandits began to enter the city to loot. The property of Wang Minglie, the head of the militia, was burned, and the county party headquarters was also burned. The Catholic Church in Goulong Lane in the city was dismantled, and Pipa Ridge, Shitang, Xiurenzai and other places were occasionally searched and looted. The flags used by the Communist bandits were disguised as the Blue Sky with a White Sun flag, and the soldiers' armbands were also like those of the party army. The clothing was quite neat, unlike the ragged clothes of those who flowed into Guangdong last year. The occupation of Shixing was led by the bandit leader Peng Dehuai, with about 4,000 people, several artillery pieces, water machine guns and hand grenades. They first extorted 100,000 yuan from the Shixing Chamber of Commerce. Since the Chamber of Commerce could not meet their demands, the Communist bandits searched house by house. Those who had grudges against them in peacetime were burned and killed. There were hundreds of propaganda teams among the Communist bandits, and there were also dozens of female propaganda teams. The slogans were mostly absurd. Until the 5th, the government troops launched a counterattack from Shao in two routes to Shixing and Renhua, and the Communist bandits decided to withdraw. On the 7th, they withdrew from Shixing and Renhua and concentrated in Nanxiong. On the same day, the Communist bandit propagandists gathered the public in Xiong City for an open-air lecture, saying that they would lead their troops to advance to Shaoguan, advising merchants to close their doors and suspend business, and that they could open their doors the next day. The merchants had to close their doors, and the road was deserted all day long. They were huddled at home, only hearing the sound of horns and the footsteps of troops moving. The next morning (the morning of the 8th), each family opened their doors, and indeed saw that all the Communist bandits had retreated. At first, they thought that the Communist bandits would attack Shaoguan, and if they were defeated and retreated to Xiong City, they would suffer. They were all on guard. Later, a husband and wife who had been recruited by the Communist bandits escaped. Curious people asked them what had happened. They said that they had been forced by the Communist bandits to carry their luggage to Dagen Ridge before finding an excuse to escape. Only then did the people of Xiong realize that the Communist bandits were feigning an attack on Shaoguan to carry out the deceitful plan of retreating to Jiangxi. After the Communist bandits withdrew, the Shaozhou Telegraph Bureau sent a telegram reporting that the Nanxiong telegram had been opened, that all the Communist bandits had completely withdrawn on the 7th, and that the order in the city was temporarily maintained by the reserve teams and that the place was safe. Wu Quan, the acting chairman of the Shixing Public Security Maintenance Association, also sent a telegram to the Eighth Route Army Headquarters and the Provincial Government, stating that, according to reliable reports, the Communist bandits who had retreated to Nanxiong had retreated from Nanxiong County City again on the morning of the 8th and fled to the Zhongzhan Dagen Ridge area, and that Nanxiong was now empty, and requested that troops be sent to maintain it, and ordered the army to track down and suppress the Communist bandits. After receiving the report, the Eighth Route Army Headquarters ordered Wu Wenxian, the commander of the Northern Jiang Bandit Suppression, to quickly send a team to maintain the security of Xiong City, and also telegraphed the Jiangxi Army to jointly encircle and suppress them. On the Guangdong side, in addition to Wu Wenxian leading six regiments to pursue Dagen Ridge, it also telegraphed Mao Weishou's Eighth Brigade in Meixian, Dongjiang, to block Longnan from Lianping. On the Jiangxi side, Division Commander Zhang Huizan also led Dai Yue, Zhu Yaohua, Cheng Guangyao, Tang Yunshan, Zhang Yuren, Deng Ying and other units to the south from Ji'an on the 5th, and launched a large-scale encirclement of the Communist bandits in southern Jiangxi. (April 12)

The Three Provincial Committee Members of Fujian Resigned 85

▲ The Five Provincial Committee Members Have Not Been Released

▲ The Provincial Government Will Have No One in Charge

Fuzhou Communication: After the Provincial Governor Yang Shuzhuang went to Shanghai on March 12, the four department heads of Civil Affairs, Finance, Education, and Construction were also absent. For a time, the Fujian Provincial Government became a political situation with no governor and no department heads. All government affairs were maintained by the three members of the Provincial Committee, Chen Peikun, Jiang Pingfan, and Lin Jinan. Recently, the three members of Chen Jianglin felt the difficulty of the provincial capital's finances, which could not be dealt with, and were forced by the rampant bandits in western Fujian, with no troops to transfer. The arrested provincial committee members had no news of release, the reorganization of the provincial government had no realization period, and Yang Shuzhuang had no definite date to return to Fujian. It was difficult to shoulder this important task. Therefore, they jointly telegraphed the National Government to resign the day before yesterday, asking them to send someone to Fujian to take over as soon as possible, and telegraphed Yang Shuzhuang, stating that they could not be responsible and asked him to return to the province to preside over it as soon as possible. After sending the telegram, Chen Peikun also claimed illness and took his family to Yongquan Temple on Gushan Mountain to recuperate, to show his determination not to do it. The situation in Fujian has become more and more shaky. Fortunately, Chen Jiliang sent someone to Gushan to persuade him with all his might, and Chen returned to the province from the mountain yesterday, but his attitude was still negative and he had not yet entered the government to work. After receiving the resignation of the three provincial committee members, Yang Shuzhuang immediately replied to comfort them, saying that he would go to Beijing to discuss the affairs of Fujian with Chairman Jiang within a few days, and then return to the province. At the same time, he sent Jiang Zhizhuang, the director of the tobacco and alcohol tax bureau who had accompanied him to Shanghai last time, back to the province on the Hua'an ship on the 11th, to personally convey Yang's advice, saying that no matter what, he should maintain the current provincial government until the end, and not put the chairman (referring to Yang Shuzhuang) in a difficult position again. However, it is said that the central government delayed the reorganization of the Fujian Provincial Government for a long time, only wanting to release the arrested provincial committee members before issuing the announcement. Now it has changed its policy and decided to reorganize the provincial government first, and then solve the release issue. Considering the past situation in Fujian Province, the candidates for the provincial committee should be independent figures who have no relationship with the military forces in the province. It is also said that Lin Sen will be sent back to Fujian to preside over it. Therefore, the political circles are rumored that Lin will return to Fujian with Liu Tong and Ding Chao Wu within a few days, but whether it is true or not remains to be seen in future reports. (April 12)

Russian Troops on the Manchurian Border Opened Fire on Us 86

▲ Two Rounds Were Fired in One Day, Shells Landed in Our Streets. Harbin Communication: The actions of the Russian troops on the Manchurian border have recently contained provocative intentions. It is not uncommon for their national defense forces to enter our borders with the passage of the Eurasian Railway and to carry weapons to roam the streets. However, on the 9th of this month, they suddenly opened fire on our territory twice. The first time was at about 5 p.m. on the 9th, and the shell landed near the East Railway Factory of Manzhouli Station, blasting the ground into a round pit. Fortunately, no one was injured. The second time was at about 9 p.m. on the 9th, and the shell landed at the western end of Toudao Street, and no one was injured because it was late. The two artillery fire sounds were extremely loud, and the merchants and residents of Manzhouli Station were extremely panicked at that time. Fortunately, the military and police authorities maintained calm and did not cause trouble. At 10 p.m. that night, Zhao, the acting representative of the Hulunbuir Diplomatic Office stationed in Manzhouli Station, invited Toyota, the Japanese consul in Manzhouli Station, and many foreigners to the landing site of the shells to inspect the situation and collect the shell casings, and asked the Japanese consul and others to prove that the Russian side had indeed opened fire on us. At 12 p.m. on the 10th, Zhao again asked the Japanese consul Toyota to visit the Russian military commander at Small Station No. 86 and ask why he opened fire on the Chinese border. The Russian military commander gave evasive answers, and finally only said that he had not heard of this matter, but said that the shells fired in the past were not fired by the Russian army, and that this time it was probably not the Russian army either. Zhao also visited the Russian consul in Manzhouli Station, who said that it was probably a military exercise and that he would telegraph the commander to inform him not to aim the cannon at the Chinese border in the future. It has been found that the Russian army also opened fire on us once on the 6th of this month. One shell landed in Bazha City of Manzhouli Station. Together with the shells fired on the 9th, it has been three times, and its intentions are very unpredictable. Also, on the 6th of this month, the Russian side sent Luo Weichi (31 years old) and Ru Qi (44 years old) into our territory to spy on military and political news. These two Russians were the main leaders in destroying traffic, setting fires and demolishing roads during the East Railway Incident last year. Our side was eager to arrest them that day, so they fled back to their country. Now they have been ordered to come to China and were captured by our Manzhouli Station police. However, the next day, the Russian consul asked for them and gave them free travel passes. The two Russians were fearless and, according to reports, have been active along the Manchurian-Hainan border into our hinterland. As for the situation on the border, since the telegraphic rights were returned to the East Railway, the news has been very insensitive to the situation in Manchuria, Hainan, and Suimu. It is necessary to wait for people to tell the story, and it takes a long time. From this, it can be seen that the Russian side is trying to win the telegraphic rights. (April 11)

Discovery of a Counter-Revolutionary Suspect Case in Liaoning 87

Shenyang Correspondence: Since the occurrence of the Anti-Imperialist Grand Alliance in Harbin, and the smashing of the International Concord Newspaper, the Northeast authorities, in addition to ordering Harbin officials to take strict precautions, immediately placed the military police of the provincial capital under invisible martial law. Searches were intensified. During the memorial service for the fallen soldiers who died in the resistance against Russia on the 5th of this month, it was suspected that troublemakers would be active during it. Fortunately, security was tight and no trouble occurred. Afterwards, the military police authorities paid even more attention. They discovered that the Second Industrial School in Xiaoheyan had a complex mix of elements. They immediately implemented a search, arresting many students and some faculty members also voluntarily resigned. Currently, the school principal has been temporarily replaced by Inspector Gao Yangzhi of the Education Department, and classes are continuing as usual. On the evening of the 12th, the National Diplomacy Association held a popular lecture. That day, Lei Gan, the Director of the Detective Division of the Gendarmerie Headquarters, received a report from his agents stating that more than twenty people had secretly arrived in Liaoning from Harbin, intending to make a statement at the External Association's lecture on the 12th. Lei led over seventy plainclothes detectives, carrying weapons, to the venue for surveillance and prevention. Just as the speaker, Wang Jinchuan, took the stage, someone suddenly jumped onto a chair in front of the stage, shouting "Down with imperialism! Down with the new warlords!" and distributing leaflets of the Anti-Imperialist Grand Alliance. As the chairman was trying to stop him, the detective team suddenly arrived. Seeing the situation was not good, the person immediately fled, but was eventually captured by the detective team. When asked about his name, he said he was Zhao Zihe, 24 years old, from Harbin, and had come to Liaoning to find Liu Butong. A search of his person revealed no incriminating evidence. Two others were arrested at the same time: a student from Northeast University named Du Lanting, and a physical education student whose name is unknown. (April 13th)

The Head of the Haizhou Gang, Zhang Zhaohua, Has Been Captured 88

Suzhou Correspondence: The Yangcheng Lake bandit gangs have been routed by the bandit suppression forces in recent days. The faction led by Zhang Zhaohua of the notorious Haizhou Gang has been completely annihilated, rescuing a total of fifty or sixty hostages. The details have been reported in this newspaper repeatedly. Now, the news obtained today will be added as follows:

▲ Gangs Routed, Bandit Leader Captured. The Haizhou Gang was divided into two factions, one led by Mao Zilong, currently entrenched in the Maoqi Port area of Taihu Lake, and the other led by Zhang Zhaohua, a combination of the Si, Chen, and Haizhou gangs. After looting Zhangyan Town in Jinshan County on the first of this month, they fled into Yangcheng Lake. The bandit suppression army first routed them at the Sanyuan Dam in Chenmu, and they fled towards the Dayao Marsh in Chefang. On the 6th, they were scattered again by the troops stationed there. Zhang Zhaohua led his followers in an attempt to flee into Taihu Lake, but then, with no way to escape, returned to the Louzitou area of Yangcheng Lake. On the 11th, Xu Boying, the captain of the 11th Water Public Security Team, surrounded and suppressed them in three routes, scattering them again. At that time, Zhang Zhaohua wanted to abandon the gang and flee, but was stopped by the gang members. On the 12th, they retreated to the Lianhua Duo in Weiting Township, and the 2nd Battalion of the 28th Bandit Suppression Regiment completely annihilated Zhang's gang. Seeing the situation was unsustainable, Zhang Zhaohua led several bandits and fled into a cave in Weiting Mountain to hide. He was discovered by Fang Yue, the captain of the patrol team stationed there, who immediately ordered the two squad leaders, Pei Xuan, to lead the team to surround them. They fired shots as a threat. Seeing the situation was not good, Zhang fled for his life, but was hit by a bullet, which entered through his buttocks and he fell to the ground wounded. He was taken back to Suzhou by the soldiers. After a brief interrogation by Captain Fang, he claimed his name was Gao Zian, and that he was Zhang Zhaohua's staff officer. After Captain Fang recorded the statement, because the bandit was seriously injured, he was sent to Guangmin Hospital for treatment. Yesterday, Squad Leader Pei went to the hospital to identify him and confirmed that the bandit was Zhang Zhaohua. The reason was that Zhang's father had been a patrol officer in the guerrilla team, and Zhang had visited his father at the team headquarters, so he recognized his face.

▲ Chief of Military Law Interrogates the Bandit Leader. After Squad Leader Pei returned to the team, he reported to Captain Fang, who then reported to the general headquarters. After General Commander Hu reported the matter, he specially sent Chief Deng of the Military Law Department and Adjutant Liu, along with Huang Houchu, the principal of the Second County Elementary School of Zhangyan Town, who was a hostage, to Guangmin Hospital to interrogate Zhang Zhaohua. He claimed to be 26 years old, from Huaiyin, and had been a soldier, then joined Mao Zilong's group as chief of staff. He did not admit to being Zhang Zhaohua. Chief Deng immediately ordered Huang Houchu to identify him, and the prisoner was indeed Zhang Zhaohua. The reason was that when Huang was kidnapped, a small leader wanted to kill him, but Zhang stopped him, saying that their purpose was only money, not his life. At that time, the bandits all called the bandit "Master Zhang" and "Brigade Commander Zhang". After Chief Deng recorded Huang Houchu's statement, he determined that the prisoner was indeed Zhang Zhaohua, but his confession was cunning and his injuries had not yet healed. He ordered the county police team to send two policemen to Guangmin Hospital to guard him and prevent him from escaping.

▲ Twenty-Six Hostages Released on Bail. The large number of hostages rescued by the military police's bandit suppression efforts were escorted from Kunshan to Suzhou on the 15th. They were taken to the Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters, and after being interrogated by the Chief of the Military Law Department, it was confirmed that they were indeed kidnapped hostages. On the 16th, they were permitted to be released on bail by their families. Those who were bailed out included Huang Houchu, Zhang Zhaoying, Gu Shijie, Zhao Weiting, Huang Weijing, Wu Lejun, Zhang Siming, Xi Chengyuan, Tao Guokang, Zhang Shouyi, Xia Wu Shi, a Jin surname female, Xia Jinlong, Xia Jiming, Guo Gechen, Guo A Nan, Guo Linsheng, Guo Zhang Shi, Pan Shu Shi, Shen Wu Shi, Shen Jingying, Shen Jingfang, Zhu Guangxian, Zhu Yinxiang, Chen Yizhang, Fan Qirui, Jiang Weiqing, and twenty others.

Mo Dehui Scheduled to Go to Russia Early Next Month 89

▲ Zhong Yu Has Officially Notified the Russian Consul in Harbin

Harbin Correspondence: Mo Dehui's trip to Russia is scheduled for May 1st. The convocation of the Sino-Russian conference will be around May 15th. Regarding the notification of the Sino-Russian conference, today (12th), Zhong Yu, the special envoy of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Harbin, personally delivered it to the Russian Consulate in Harbin at noon, handing it to the Russian Consul Melnikov in person. There were Chinese and Russian versions of the notification, and the content was very simple, roughly stating: "The Chinese government hereby appoints Mo Dehui, the Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway, as the plenipotentiary representative for the Sino-Soviet Conference, scheduled to depart on May 1st to Moscow to convene the Sino-Soviet Conference. This is a notification, hoping that you will forward it to your government." The Russian Consul stated at the time that he would telegraph it to his country's government, and that a reply would arrive in Harbin in about a week, at which time he would forward it again. The notification took a lot of time to research and draft, partly because it was to prevent the Russian side from refusing to accept it, so the wording was carefully considered several times. On the morning of the 11th, the original text was telegraphed to the Northeast Political Committee, and after discussion, a reply was sent in the evening approving it. It was only sent out today. In addition to Li Chen of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Tu Weizeng of the Ministry of Railways, and Sun Guangdou, a newly appointed consul in Shuangchengzi, who will serve as translators, the rest of Mo's entourage has not yet been decided. (April 12th)

Since the price of rice has soared in the urban and rural areas of this county, people from the middle and lower classes commonly feel the difficulty of living. Ningbo 101

Two Robbery Cases. At the home of Yao Sun Shi, an old woman in Yunlongzhen, Yin County, six robbers suddenly broke in last night, ransacking chests and cabinets, and stealing two gold rings, a pair of gold bracelets, twenty-seven silver dollars, and clothes. The old woman went outside to shout, and was beaten on the head by the robbers, causing serious injuries. Also, in the Chen Liuqiu Village on the lake embankment in Xixiang, Yuyao, nine robbers suddenly broke into the home of resident Lin Rong yesterday afternoon, stealing a gold bracelet, several gold rings, a pair of gold bracelets, several leather jackets, and over a hundred paper dollars. Lin Rong fought with the robbers and was slashed on the knee, and the robbers fled.

The Resignation of the Public Security Bureau Chief Has Been Approved. Mao Bingli, the chief of the Ningbo Municipal Public Security Bureau, has resigned due to difficulties in handling affairs. According to news from a certain organization, the province has approved Chief Mao's resignation, and it has been internally decided to appoint Liu Zuhan, the former director of the Liangzhe Anti-Smuggling Bureau, to succeed him.

A Prodigal Son Remarries; Father Dies of Anger, Wife Hangs Herself. Fang Zizhen, from Zhushan Bridge in Cibai, Cixi, married Ye Shi from the same village several years ago. Half a month after their marriage, he went to Japan and never returned for several years. His father repeatedly urged him to return home, but to no avail. A letter suddenly arrived from Tokyo a few days ago, saying that Zizhen had remarried to a Japanese woman and asked to divorce Ye Shi, otherwise he would never return home. His father, who suffered from asthma, was furious when he saw the letter, and his phlegm blocked his breath, causing him to die. His wife, Ye Shi, after her father-in-law's funeral, looked around at the silent walls and, unable to live on and with no home to return to, hanged herself from a tree.

A Maiden Defiled, Commits Suicide by Poison. Sanqiu, on the north side of Xinpu, Yuyao, is a remote and sparsely populated place. There is a farmer, Gao Binfang, and his wife, Mei Shi, both in their fifties, with only one daughter, nineteen years old, named Liqing, who is beautiful, virtuous, and fond of reading in her spare time. Her parents love her as the apple of their eye. However, the other day, the Gao couple went out to sweep the tombs and asked their daughter to guard the house. After the Gao couple left, their daughter was bored at home and stood outside the door for a while. Unexpectedly, an evil young man suddenly appeared and raped her. Overwhelmed with shame and indignation, the girl took poison and tried to end her life. When her parents returned from sweeping the tombs, she was already barely breathing.

Xinghua 102

Xinghua County Disaster Asks for Relief. Xingyi suffered from locusts and drought last year, and the crops failed. The old and weak filled the ditches, and the young and strong flowed to all sides. Such a great disaster is a rare famine unseen in decades. Local people have tried their best, but it is just a drop in the bucket. Although winter relief was barely completed, spring relief is even more urgent. Wei Chonggeng and others from the Xingdai Boy Scout Service Team are going to Beijing to participate in the National Boy Scout Review. The Relief Branch Committee specially entrusts them to promote donations to comrades from various provinces and counties participating in the review, in order to maintain it, and also sends a letter to the National Boy Scout Review Preparatory Office to assist.

Wuyuan 103

Rare Hailstorm in Wuyuan. The weather in Wuyuan has been unusually hot and sultry for several days. Last night (7th) at 9 p.m., there was thunder and lightning, a howling gale, and a sudden hailstorm. Fortunately, it lasted only a few hours. The large hailstones were the size of chicken eggs, and the small ones were the size of broad beans. Pedestrians could not avoid them and were mostly injured. The most severe damage occurred in Sixi, Yancun, Datian Duan, Hegong, Linchun, Licun, Daicun in the northern countryside, and Fuchun in the western countryside. One person was struck and killed by lightning in Licun, and four people were crushed to death by collapsing houses in Fuchun. Two people were crushed to death by collapsing houses in Yancun. The losses in each village are estimated at one thousand to several thousand yuan. The losses in other villages have not been investigated, but the damage is likely to be significant. The number of trees, tea, wheat, thatched houses, and brick walls that were crushed, broken, or damaged is countless. Along the main roads, large trees were uprooted and lying across the road everywhere, blocking traffic. According to the elders in the county, the magnitude of this wind and hailstorm and the extent of the disaster are unseen in over a hundred years. The total losses are at least over 200,000 yuan.

Hefei 104

Robbery and Murder Case Occurs in a Busy Market. The Hengshunlong Money Shop on Dongmen Main Street, which exchanges silver dollars and banknotes, is opened by twin brothers Li Shouzhong and Shouhe. In September of last year, robbers robbed the shop, and Shouhe was shot to death with a handgun while resisting. The case has not been solved to this day. Unexpectedly, at 7 p.m. on the 9th, Shouzhong opened the iron cabinet and counted a large number of banknotes because a certain money shop had an agreement to exchange 4,000 yuan in banknotes on the 10th. At that time, eight robbers, each carrying a box gun, broke into the shop and grabbed the banknotes from the open iron cabinet. Shouzhong, unable to resist, withdrew and went outside, shouting to catch the robbers. The robbers who were acting as lookouts outside shot him twice in a row, hitting him in vital spots. He soon died. The robbers also fled in a crowd through Fuxing Lane. When Li's wife heard the alarm and came out to look, and reported it to the Merchant Corps to arrest them, they had already disappeared without a trace. After checking, it was estimated that 3,400 yuan in paper dollars had been robbed.

County Court to Be Established by Deadline. Yang Changchi, the preparator for the Hefei County Court, has been in Hefei for more than a month, but due to the issue of building funds and location, he has been unable to start. Now, because the Higher Court has telegraphed an order that it must be established by May 1st, Committee Member Yang urgently urged the county government to allocate funds and selected the east side of the county government as the court site, and construction will begin within days.

Meeting Place Arrangement 107

The meeting place arrangement was slightly different from yesterday. The southeast and southwest corners were still reserved for the press. The chairman's platform faced north, with the stenography and record-keeping desks for the conference in front. The seating for the 144 members was assigned by the conference committee in a specific order. Starting from the westernmost seat of the southernmost row, it was designated as number one, with the seat to its east as number two. From there, the numbers were assigned eastward, up to number sixteen. The first seat of the second row was number seventeen, and the rest followed in a similar fashion. In front of each seat, the conference committee placed a blank name card with the seat number written on it for identification. North of the members' seats were the spectator seats, arranged in four rows of iron chairs, totaling sixty seats. On each member's seat, two pencils and several sheets of lined paper were provided for note-taking.

Conference Proceedings 108

The meeting commenced promptly at nine o'clock in the morning. First, Chairman Chiang Monlin, the Minister, reverently read Premier Sun Yat-sen's will. Then, he announced that Mr. Li Shizeng would deliver a speech.

Li Shizeng's Speech 109

The year before last, I was abroad and therefore did not participate in the first conference. Those attending this session are all academic and educational experts. Therefore, my presence here allows me to express my simplest personal thoughts. My thoughts carry a sense of deliberation. Within the universe, time and space are limited, thus giving rise to various problems. In essence, these are merely different forms of A, B, C, D, etc. The limitations of time and space are exemplified in many historical instances. Taking China's recent education and knowledge into consideration, the state of education and knowledge thirty or forty years ago is vastly different from the state of education and knowledge today. Thirty or forty years ago, the thinking of 80% of the farmers was similar to the thinking of farmers today. However, in terms of education and knowledge, the difference between thirty or forty years ago and today is significant. Therefore, to promote education effectively, a relatively small number of people should take on the task of ensuring that 80% to 90% of farmers become literate, as a crucial endeavor. Since then, various cultural changes have led to the era of new culture and new education today. This so-called new era, based on various observations, analyses, and studies, is naturally different from the past. Generally, from a psychological perspective, people are pursuing novelty. One day, I was discussing Eastern and Western cultures with a friend, and we agreed that most Chinese people view Chinese culture as old and Western culture as new. In reality, there is no such thing as new or old; the only question is whether it is suitable. We do not expect Eastern culture to be transferred to the West, or Western culture to be transferred to the East. In terms of education, we must not simply transplant foreign systems and methods to our country without considering whether they are suitable for our national circumstances. Yesterday, Mr. Wu Zhihui raised the issue of writing. We can use this to explain the issue of Eastern and Western cultures. The world's writing systems have evolved from inconvenient to convenient ones. The evolution of Chinese writing is different. Chinese people strive for the beauty of their written characters. This mentality is more prevalent in our country than in foreign countries. Chinese writing is artistic, while Western writing emphasizes application. From this, we can understand the difference between Eastern and Western cultures. Some people genuinely advocate the romanization of Chinese characters. In fact, Chinese characters should not only not be abolished, but their unique strengths should be preserved. This is not about clinging to the old ways of the East, but because writing, besides being a tool for application and art, also involves historical issues. No other writing system in the world has been passed down for 5,000 years like Chinese characters. Therefore, the romanization of Chinese characters can be regarded as an auxiliary tool, but it should not be seen as the primary tool. Some believe that Chinese characters are difficult to learn and write. I believe that this situation is not a problem. In various countries around the world, farmers from wealthy families often own pianos to cultivate their emotional well-being. This is similar to the time spent by Chinese people in writing beautiful characters. We should not hastily regard Chinese characters as a difficult problem. Today, Eastern culture is being introduced to the West, and Western culture is being introduced to the East, leading to the emergence of a new culture. Neither Eastern culture nor Western culture will be eliminated. If there were only Western culture without Eastern culture, then this Western culture would become the culture of imperialism. There is also a social issue that can be discussed together. Recently, Chinese youth have believed that those who do not read Marxist books are backward. Little do they know that this ideology, which uses struggle as a means, is actually an old aspect of Western culture and is no match for the Three Principles of the People, which starts with love and is new. I sincerely hope that future education will produce genuinely innovative education that is suitable for our country and promote it throughout our nation.

Therefore, it was appropriate to hold a large meeting during the conference for detailed discussion to achieve excellence and perfection. Education Group Begins Review of Education Plan 116

After the Education Plan was submitted by the Central Political Council to the Education Group for review, the Education Group began its review after the Central Political Council adjourned on the 16th. Because the full text of the case was too long, it was not possible to complete the review in one sitting and planned to continue the review from the 17th onwards.

Review Overview 117

▲Adult Remedial Group

Review results of the Adult Remedial Education Group: (1) Changed Adult Remedial Education to People's Remedial Education, (2) Added civic training to the goals, (3) National Literacy Schools were renamed People's Schools, (4) The Three Principles of the People Thousand-Character Lesson was changed to the Three Principles of the People Lesson, (5) Educationally affiliated private groups should vigorously promote People's Education, and the rest were passed.

▲Compulsory Education Group

Review results of the Compulsory Education Group: (1) In the original target item (but for poor children in rural or urban areas), it was changed to any child who cannot continue in school for four years, (2) Under the original deadline item, the national uniform implementation of four years of compulsory education was added, but the chief education officials of each city may shorten the period or advance the completion of this task in accordance with local conditions, (3) Under the original notes six items, temporarily set from six to twelve years old sentence, add (if necessary may be extended to fifteen years old) eleven words, put in parentheses, then connect the deadline is shorter than Europe and the United States, the secondary education review report principle, the first secondary education must comply with the national education purpose, the second (general education must be based on Premier Sun's last teachings, cultivate children and youth's loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, justice, peace of national morality, and cultivate the national life skills, enhance the national productive capacity as the main purpose, to cultivate solid and sound citizens under the rule of the Party, the second should be based on the high and junior high schools each unique function, training group life, identification of student personality, adapt to social needs, prepare for higher education, formulate various facilities, in order to achieve the practice, the national education purpose, our country's secondary education quantity and quality, compared to the world's advanced countries, is far inferior, we should actively improve and promote, but during the period of political training, compulsory education and adult remedial education, are particularly urgent, the required funding is very large, consider the financial resources, we must divide the priorities, so at present secondary education, can only be reorganized on the basis of existing schools, the progress of quality, vocational training, should also pay attention to the improvement of quality, as for the increase in quantity, can only take a gradual approach, and expand in stages.

▲Elementary Education Group

Review results of the Elementary Education Group: (1) In terms of establishment, deleted the original provision that groups not fully organized by the Chinese people may not establish elementary schools or kindergartens, (2) In terms of economics, the original provision that the proportion of salaries and wages in the operating expenses should not exceed 75% was changed to 80%, (3) Under construction and equipment, added that the standards for general equipment in small kindergartens should be determined by the education departments of each province themselves, and the table books should also be determined by each department, and the rest were largely passed.

▲Overseas Chinese Education Group

Review results of the Overseas Chinese Education Group: (1) In terms of organization, requested that the Ministry of Education quickly establish an Overseas Chinese Education Department, and before the addition, a senior ministry member should be appointed to specifically handle Overseas Chinese Education affairs and assign cadres to go to the residence of overseas Chinese to inspect, (2) In terms of funding, raise 3 million yuan for the fund within one year, the central government raises 2 million, Guangdong raises 600,000, Fujian raises 400,000, and then raise 7 million yuan within six years, (3) In terms of the implementation of school education, the Ministry of Education should give special awards to overseas Chinese who donate to establish schools, (4) Temporary motion case, appointed Committee Member Zhuang Zexuan to draft a fundamental remedy for the recent economic failures of overseas Chinese: (A) The government should first pay import duties on important products produced in the overseas Chinese location and transported to China, (B) The Ministry of Industry and Commerce should add industry and commerce commissioners to the overseas Chinese location to assist the development of the industry and commerce of overseas Chinese, (C) The Ministry of Education should designate universities related to overseas Chinese to train overseas Chinese affairs cadres.

In the early stage of political training, it is especially important. We should follow the comrades of the Central Training Department and strive to develop in the direction of people's livelihood, so that education can have good results. Taking agricultural education as an example, we should not only implement agricultural education training, but also promote it to the society to seek benefits for the people's livelihood. Furthermore, in the future, China's education should not only promote new knowledge, but also develop and promote old culture. Mr. Li Shizeng said at the conference today that old culture and new culture are not contradictory. No matter how Chinese education develops in new directions, old culture should be preserved for a considerable period of time. We are willing to make continuous efforts for Chinese education to respond to the warm hospitality of the Central Training Department and hope that you will give us your kind guidance. The dinner lasted for two hours, and the guests and hosts dispersed in joy.

The Academia Sinica held a public banquet to welcome the members of the conference and show their sincerity. The location was the Arctic Geophysics Institute. The preparation of this location started in the autumn of 1927. On January 1, 1928, observations began on the remaining land of the University Council Garden on Chengxian Street. The buildings of the Arctic Geophysics Institute were completed in January 1929, and then the office was moved in. The house is high, facing the back lake to the north, the air is fresh, and the scenery is pleasant, making it a great place to study academics. Members gathering here for a banquet will have a different flavor than the banquet at the First Park on the 15th.
