Ma Chuntai, a Primary School Student from Biwen, Kidnapped 155

▲ Left Home in the Afternoon, Disappeared

▲ Received a Letter from the Bandits Yesterday, Discovering the Kidnapping

▲ Due to a Grudge with His Father, They Kidnapped His Son

▲ Ransom of 500 Yuan Required for Release

The six-year-old boy from the Ma De Ji Clothing Store on Fang Xie Road in Nanshi disappeared the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, a letter was suddenly received, revealing that he had been kidnapped by bandits. The details are as follows:

▲ Old Shop with a Reputation: Ma Ji, a native of Changzhou, is 36 years old and has been running the Ma De Ji Clothing Store at No. 332 Baolong Lane, near Baiyun Temple on Fang Xie Road in Nanshi, for over 20 years. It was founded by Ma's father, Jin Gao. In addition to his own work, Ma employs several partners and apprentices. His monthly income is just enough to make ends meet. Ma's wife, Sun, is 35 years old and has only one son, six-year-old Chuntai. The child is naturally clever and was sent to Biwen Girls' School at No. 104 Xilinhou Road nearby when he was five years old.

▲ Sudden Disappearance: Chuntai usually goes to school with several neighbors every morning. The school provides lunch, and school ends at 5:00 PM. It was the usual routine. At 11:00 AM the day before yesterday, he returned home for lunch. His mother told him to wait a moment because the meal was not yet ready. After the meal, he left with his neighbors again and returned to ask Sun for three copper coins. At the same time, Sun also went to relatives in Yangshupu for business. When she returned home at 6:00 PM, she found that Chuntai had not yet returned home. She went to the school to inquire and was told by the teacher that he had not returned to school after lunch. The whole family was in a panic, suspecting that he was missing. They immediately sent out search parties.

▲ Suddenly Received a Letter from the Bandits: Ma was distraught over the disappearance of his son and sent out search parties to search all night, but there was no trace of him. At about 9:00 AM yesterday, Ma suddenly received a letter, which stated that they had a long-standing grudge with him, so they had hidden his son. If he wanted his son back, he had to pay 500 yuan. The letter also arranged a meeting place near the Sun Temple in Chubei. After receiving the letter, Ma did not dare to report it to the police at the time. However, Zhang Heshan, the patrol chief of the Second District, passed by and heard people talking about it. He reported it to District Chief Wang. District Chief Wang immediately sent Inspector Gao Hongbin to investigate.

▲ Ordered a Crackdown: When Inspector Gao went to investigate, Ma initially concealed the truth. After he told the truth, Inspector Gao took the letter from the bandits to the police station and reported it to District Chief Wang. After receiving the report, District Chief Wang immediately ordered the team leader of the detectives, Cao Junda, and the detectives on duty to strictly investigate the case. If the bandits could repent and send Chuntai back, they would not be investigated further. If they remained unrepentant and insisted on extortion, they would not be tolerated once they were caught. By then, it would be too late to regret it.

Four Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad 156

▲ Six Involved in the Same Case

▲ Two Sent Back for Retrial

▲ The Four Criminals Protested Before Their Deaths

▲ Why Aren't the Other Two Dying Too?

▲ Brutally Killed Ye Daming: The kidnappers Wang Liangui, Li Afu, Rong Zhengchang, Shen Shaoqing, Ma Qiyuan, and Liu Fuxing (also known as Wang Laosi), etc., kidnapped Ye Zhuotang's son, Ye Daming, on Kade Road in Huxi on May 31st of last year. Because he resisted, the bandits brutally killed him.

▲ Committed Two More Kidnappings: Later, they were arrested by the police and found to have also kidnapped Chu Pusun, chairman of the Gold Exchange on Nanjing Road, and Ni Yugui, manager of the Shenxin Yarn Factory on Bailinan Road, for ransom. In addition, they committed multiple robberies.

▲ Two Criminals Must Be Retried: The former Provisional Court investigated and sentenced the six bandits, including Wang, to death and reported it to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for review. Now, the order has been issued to the court. Except for Ma and Liu, who were sent back for retrial, the rest will be executed according to the judgment.

▲ Saying Goodbye to Their Mothers: At 2:00 PM yesterday, the Special District District Court notified the police station to escort the four criminals, Wang, Li, Rong, and Shen, to the Third Tribunal. Presiding Judge Cheng Shangfeng ascended the bench, announced the provincial order, and asked the criminals if they had any last words. Wang Liangui stated that his other name was Wang Chaolin, he was 28 years old, a native of Wuxi, and lived at No. 2464 behind the court in Shanghai. He still had parents and brothers at home. He was a carpenter. He had three long gowns, a fur coat, and a raincoat when he was arrested and requested that they be returned. His mother was also in court and asked to be allowed to see her one last time. The judge granted permission, and Wang spoke a few words with his mother.

▲ Pretending to Be Calm: Li Afu then stated that his other name was Tang Jinbiao, he was 40 years old, a native of Ningbo, and lived at No. 721 Fuxu Road in Shanghai. He had no last words. Rong Zhengchang stated that his other name was Xiao Rong, he was from Wuxi, and lived in Zhoujiaqiao. He specialized in kidnapping. He asked to send a letter to the Cloth Room of the Housheng Yarn Factory on Lan Road to his brother, Rong Yueqing, so that he would know that he had been executed today. He pretended to be calm while speaking.

▲ Twenty Years Is Still a Young Man: Shen Shaoqing stated that he was 31 years old, a local, and used to be a chauffeur at No. 202 Fukaissen Road, nicknamed Xiao Shen. Since he had committed the crime of kidnapping, he should be executed. In twenty years, he would still be a young man.

▲ Protesting at the Last Minute: Wang, Li, Rong, and Shen then stated that Ma and Liu were actually informants in the Ye Daming kidnapping case. If they had not reported it, how would they have known that Ye was wealthy? Therefore, their deaths were actually caused by Ma and Liu. Since the two were sentenced to death at the same time, why were only the four of them being sent for execution today? Judge Cheng replied that the provincial government had ordered that the cases of Ma and Liu be reviewed, so they could not be executed today.

▲ The Cries of the Families: After the order was given, the four criminals were ordered to board the car, along with the judgment and photos, and were handed over to the detectives for escort to the Jiangxi Second Prison execution ground in Caohejing. The Shanghai District Court was also entrusted to send a prosecutor and execution police officers to the scene to verify their identities and order the execution. Police Chief Yang directed the police officers to take the four criminals down and execute them together by firing squad. Gunshots rang out, and the families of the executed criminals outside the gate cried loudly. After the inspecting officer verified that each criminal was dead, he ordered that they be temporarily taken for coffin and sealing, waiting for the family members to claim them. Although the Shanghai District Court's Special Zone Court's equipment was gradually being completed, the death penalty must be carried out by the court itself. However, the Special Zone Court had not yet prepared all the procedures for carrying out the death penalty, so this time it still relied on the police officers of the District Court to handle the matter.

A Scavenger Finds a Bomb 158

▲ Mistook It for a Valuable Item

▲ Blew Off Half of His Finger

Xu Fulin, a native of Wuxi, is 39 years old and makes a living by scavenging. Yesterday morning at 5:00 AM, he found a bomb wrapped in paper under the corridor on the west side of the intersection of Zilai Street and the main road in the French Concession. Xu did not know what it was at first, mistaking it for a valuable item. After picking it up, he took it to the front of No. 25 Jixing Lane, Jixiang Street, and opened the package to examine it. There was a glass tube on top of the bomb. Xu tried to pull out the glass tube. As soon as he moved it, it suddenly exploded with a loud bang and flames spread everywhere, instantly blowing off the upper half of Xu's right finger. Blood and flesh flew everywhere, and he fainted and fell to the ground. The police heard the sound and rushed to the scene. After questioning him, the police chief ordered him to be sent to Renji Hospital for treatment pending further investigation.

Strange Death of a Female Worker at the Yong'an Yarn Factory 159

▲ Body Prostrate as If Praying to Buddha

▲ Thin Oiled Yarn Around Her Neck

Ding Caier, an 18-year-old female worker from Qinzhou at the Yong'an Second Yarn Factory in Wusong Yanzao, who lived in the No. 91 workshop of Yong'an, suddenly hanged herself yesterday morning at 6:00 AM for unknown reasons. Her roommates found out and broke into the room to rescue her, but it was too late. Housing Dispute in Yin Yu Lane Resolved 160

▲ Rent Reduction of 10 to 15 Yuan

▲ No Increase or Decrease Within Four Years

The houses in the Yin Yu Lane area of ​​the French Concession were renovated last year by the British firm Dehe Foreign Company, which also acted as the rental agent. Construction began around last summer and was completed in August and September. There are more than 100 houses inside and outside. The price of housing is 65 to 70 yuan per building, and the price of market houses is 90 to 130 yuan. The total monthly income is 8,000 to 9,000 yuan, which is much higher than the monthly income of 2,000 yuan before the renovation. The old tenants complained that the rent had increased three or four times, and they could not afford it. They formed the "Yin Yu Lane Tenants' Union" and repeatedly sent letters requesting the landlord and the comprador of Dehe Foreign Company to reduce the rent slightly to accommodate the public. The dispute lasted for two or three months, but there was still no solution. They hired lawyer Zheng Yuxiu to prepare legal action. On one hand, the tenants automatically deposited the rent into the China Bank in Baxianqiao. On the other hand, the General Union of Tenants of the French Concession sent a written warning to the landlord. Later, Yu Qiaqing and Shang Mu Jiang came forward to mediate. After repeated consultations, they agreed to reduce the rent for market houses by 10 to 15 yuan and the rent for residential houses by 8 to 9 yuan. There would be no increase or decrease within four years from the date of the lease. The reply letter from Yu was received yesterday, and Lawyer Zheng stamped it to certify it and took 100 photos to distribute to the tenants for safekeeping. All unpaid rent will be collected in the name of Yin Ji. The tenants' representatives also resolved at a meeting: (1) The name of the Yin Yu Lane Tenants' Union will be preserved forever. (2) More than a dozen large and small silver shields will be made and given to Yu, Shang, Wang, Chen, Zhu, and Wei and others who contributed to the effort. (3) Representatives will be invited to a celebration banquet on a certain day to report on the progress. (4) A notice of thanks will be published in the newspaper to Yu and Shang and the General Union of Tenants of the French Concession for their assistance. (5) Chairpersons and other executive officers will be elected by the Representative Council to handle union affairs. (6) The 10% public fee collected has not been used and will be permanently deposited in the China Bank for emergencies.

Municipal Bureau of Public Works Plans Routes 161

▲ Xiangzha Road: Since the Municipal Government determined the downtown area, the Bureau of Public Works has been planning various routes. The Xiangzha Road starts from Diswei Road, uses the entire line of Yangjiabang Road in the Zhabei District road system, crosses the Shajing Port, passes Chenjiazha, Hongjiazha, and ends at the intersection of Xiangyin Road and Songhu Road. The entire road is more than five kilometers long and is a main road connecting the downtown area to the concession. It is now reported that the Municipal Bureau of Public Works has completed the route plan. The width of the road is stipulated to be 35 meters from Shajing Port to Xiangyin Road. The original width of Yangjiabang Road, 15.3 meters, will be maintained west of Shajing Port to Diswei Road. However, the baseline on both sides is still set at 35 meters so that when traffic increases in the future and the original width is insufficient, it can still be widened without the difficulty of demolishing houses.

▲ Yanpu Road: The original roads along the outer Bund of the 16th Pier of Damada Wharf and the Datong Wharf south of Dongjiadu were of varying widths. Goods were piled up along the road, and vehicles could not pass. The traffic on the outer Bund was becoming increasingly congested. Now, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works plans to take advantage of the city's reorganization of the Yanpu coastline and public land to plan the route from the 16th Pier to Dongjiadu in detail, so that vehicles for wharves and warehouses can use the road for parking in the future, thereby reducing congestion on the outer Bund and benefiting traffic. The bureau has drawn a detailed map of the route and submitted it to the municipal government for review and approval. The segment of the road near Pu浜 has been submitted to the Municipal Council meeting for decision and is stipulated to be 93 meters wide.

Special District Court Issues Audience Tickets 164

▲ Those Unrelated Are Not Allowed to Enter the Court

▲ One Ticket Limited to One Court

Because during the daily hearings of civil and criminal cases in the Special District Court, unrelated non-litigants often intrude into the court, it has become necessary to slightly restrict access. Therefore, starting yesterday, anyone wishing to attend must obtain an audience ticket. The ticket is specially made by the court with a white background and red characters, marked with the court number, "Audience Ticket," the date, and "Void After One Day." The bailiffs or court clerks of each court are responsible for issuing the tickets. The bailiffs will first inquire about the case and the relationship of the person attending, and then issue an audience ticket. If it is found that the person is completely unrelated, they will not be given a ticket and will be barred from the court. Moreover, since the ticket has the court number printed on it, it is not allowed to use a ticket from Court A to enter Court B. When leaving, the ticket holders must return the original ticket to prevent misuse. The Special District Court has five civil courts and five criminal courts, so if all ten courts are open every day, nearly a thousand audience tickets will be needed. At the very least, it will be more than five hundred. Calculated over the whole year, the cost will be considerable. It is said that the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court will also implement this method, which can reduce the chaos in the courtroom during trial proceedings.

America's Tallest Wireless Radio Station Building 166

▲ Music Can Be Received in Various Ports in the Far East

According to American sources in this city, the American Radio Company is building a new building, fifty stories high, located at the intersection of Lexington Avenue and East 21st Street. It is expected to be completed by mid-May next year. The building is in the style of an ancient church, with a spire towering into the clouds. A wireless radio station is installed on top of the spire, making it the tallest in the world. At night, the top of the spire is illuminated with colorful electric lights, which is extremely brilliant and represents the spirit of wireless radio. After the new building is completed, most of it will be used as offices for the American Radio Company, with a grand scale. It is said that the construction cost is approximately several million yuan or more. When it is completed in the future, music will be broadcast, and it can be received in various ports in the Far East.

Verdict in the Yan Ruling Kidnapping Case 168

▲ Seven Criminals Sentenced to Five Years Each

▲ Sent to Mainland Court for Punishment

Yan Ruling, the comprador of the former French and Chinese Oriental Fur Company, was kidnapped by bandits some time ago in his new house on Route Lafayette and taken to a bandit den in a foreign house at No. 356 Jin Shenfu Road. Later, detective inspector Jin Jiulin and chief detective Li Yaolong of the French police station discovered the den, rescued the victim, and arrested the kidnappers Zhang Hongxiang, Lu Peizhou, Wang A'gen, Fang Youshan, Tao Jinbao, Luo Shisheng, Chen Liangen, Wang A'da, and the suspect Zhao Renmao, a total of nine people. Three pistols and one Mauser pistol were seized. The details of the interrogation in the French Public Court have been recorded in previous reports. Yesterday, they were brought in for questioning again. According to Zhang Hongxiang and others, the driver Wang A'gen did indeed help drive the car during the kidnapping of the plaintiff. The plaintiff's representative, lawyer Ba He, stated that the kidnappers in the case have all admitted their guilt without denial. It was found that the second defendant, Lu Peizhou, is a relative of the plaintiff. The plaintiff's kidnapping was entirely instigated by Lu alone, who had led the accomplices to the new house to identify the plaintiff's appearance. He had also conspired with the gang to kidnap his brother, Liu Chengxiao, and Qian Changgan, etc. last year. At a time when kidnapping is rampant and the social atmosphere is deteriorating, the court should severely punish them to deter lawbreakers. At this point, the Chinese and Western officials ordered Zhang Fuqing to be brought to court and asked, "Do you owe your cousin Zhang Hongxiang 400 yuan and eight rickshaws? If so, you can return them to his wife to help her make a living." Zhang Fuqing replied, "I have been working as a detective in the mainland. Zhang Hongxiang was once arrested by me, so he falsely accused me out of resentment. I do not owe him a penny. Moreover, Zhang Hongxiang's money was obtained by kidnapping and risking his life. If I were to covet this money, my heart would be ten times more vicious than his. Please investigate." The official asked Zhang Hongxiang if he had any loan receipts. Zhang replied that he had no receipts. Presiding Judge Zhu then consulted with French Consul Du and sentenced Zhang Hongxiang, Lu Peizhou, Wang A'gen, Fang Youshan, Tao Jinbao, Luo Shisheng, and Chen Liangen, seven people in total, to five years in the Western prison for the crime of violating Article 371 of the criminal law, to be deported and sent to the mainland court for punishment. Wang A'da was sentenced to five years and deported. The seized pistols and Mauser pistol were confiscated. Zhao Renmao was released as he was not involved.

Female Corpse Retrieved from Wusong Seashore 171

A female corpse was found floating on the seashore east of the Wusong Fort yesterday morning at around 7:00 AM. The local bailiff, Zhang A'mao, retrieved the corpse and reported it to the Baoshan County Government. County Magistrate Wu dispatched personnel at 1:00 PM to inspect the body. It was found that the corpse was about 30 years old, with no injuries on the body. She was wearing blue cloth shirt and pants, barefoot, and had nothing in her pockets. After the inspection, the county government prepared a coffin and collected the body, waiting for her family to identify it.

Shandong Boy Lost in Shanghai 172

A Shandong boy named Liu Xiaozhu, 13 years old, used to live in Qingdao. Because his mother died early, his father remarried. Recently, his father's livelihood has become increasingly difficult, so he joined the army. His stepmother is inherently fierce and often beats him. Liu, unable to bear the abuse, secretly ran away. The day before yesterday, he came to Shanghai by boat. After landing, he planned to go to his aunt's husband, Zhang Qiangzhen's, grocery store near the South Railway Station. However, he did not know the way and wandered around Wangjia Wharf in Nanshi. Later, he remembered that there was an old people's home in Shanghai that could take him in, so he asked the guard at the 15th post where the address was. The policeman knew that something was wrong and inquired about his background. He took him back to the First Branch of the First District and was ordered to submit a written report to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for placement.

Jiangxi Province Temporarily Suspends Foreign Travel 173

The Shanghai Special Municipal Government recently approved a consultation from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, approving a telegram from the Jiangxi Provincial Government stating that the province is currently conducting a large-scale suppression of bandits. It is inconvenient for foreigners to travel to Jiangxi. The ministry is requested to instruct all passport-issuing agencies to temporarily suspend the issuance of passports. Those who have already obtained passports are requested to be notified not to lightly travel to unstable areas to avoid danger and show due caution, etc. Upon approval, in addition to sending consultations to various provincial governments for information, a corresponding letter is sent to you for your review and to instruct your subordinates to comply, etc. It is said that after receiving the consultation, the municipal government has already ordered the Public Security Bureau to comply with the instructions.

Two People Attempt Suicide by Poisoning 174

▲ Woman in Critical Condition, Man Unharmed

Shen Zhongtao, from Zhenjiang, residing at 453 Ziyang Lane, Huishan Road, used to work as a partner at Jiu Kang Cloth Store in his hometown. Later, due to the closure of the store, he brought his wife, Yin, to Shanghai last year, hoping to find a business. However, he was unsuccessful and has been unemployed ever since. All their clothes and ornaments have been pawned. Although Ms. Yin was recommended to work as a female worker at the Huaping Cigarette Factory, and is a novice, her income is meager and insufficient to cover expenses. Quarrels are often heard in the family. Yesterday morning, the couple quarreled again. Ms. Yin, feeling depressed, secretly took opium paste to end her life. Shen discovered it and accompanied her to the Civilian Hospital, then transferred her to Tongren Hospital for treatment. It is said that her life is in danger.

Sun Yuanli, a Ningbo native, 42 years old, lives at 901 Ou Pengjia Road, Hongkou. His son, Qingmiao, 20 years old, used to serve on Yangtze River ships. Because he was addicted to gambling, he was dismissed and worked as a clerk in his father's Meili Dyeing Workshop (492 Qiujiang Road, Zhabei). Recently, he relapsed into his old habits and lost a lot of money. His father discovered this and severely reprimanded him. In a fit of frustration, Qingmiao secretly took raw opium to kill himself at around 4:00 PM yesterday. He was discovered and hired a streetcar to send him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Because the poisoning was mild, he was unharmed.

A Laughing Matter 175

— Sea Traveler

▲ Housewife: You thieving beggar! Get out of here! Otherwise, I'll call my husband to beat you!

Beggar: Heh! Don't try to fool me. Your husband isn't home.

Housewife: How do you know he's not home?

Beggar: Because any man who marries a shrew like you will only come home to eat and sleep. He definitely won't be home at other times.

▲ Girl A: You say she married out of love this time, but I heard her husband is an old man with 500,000 yuan in assets.

Girl B: Of course! What she loves is the 500,000 yuan in assets.

▲ Gentleman: My child, how old are you?

Child: My age isn't fixed. Normally, I'm ten years old. But when I ride the tram with my mother, I become six years old.

▲ Woman A: You say brandy can cure heatstroke, but I don't think so. On the contrary, it causes heatstroke.

Woman B: Why?

Woman A: Because before I had brandy, my husband never had heatstroke. But since I bought two bottles of Three-Star Brandy recently, he has heatstroke every day.

▲ Gardener: What are you doing hiding in my apple tree?

Apple Thief: I just fell out of an airplane.

Dr. Chu's Notes on Overseas Anecdotes 176

— Xu Shiqi

Mr. Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, is known for promoting hygiene education. This time, he represented the country in Belgium. I was sent to Europe by the Ministry and set off on the same ship. I had the opportunity to personally listen to his teachings. Besides teaching French and practicing Tai Chi on the Astor ship every day, Mr. Chu also narrated his experiences in Europe endlessly. Here are some of his overseas anecdotes to share with readers.

▲ Language Master The most popular languages in the world are English, German, and French. The Americas and Australia have the same language, which has a wider scope. Therefore, Americans and British people who can speak more than two languages are very rare. People in countries such as Poland, Denmark, Switzerland, and the Netherlands can often understand more than ten languages. Therefore, language masters should belong to small European countries.

▲ Truth, Goodness, and Beauty Our physical health depends entirely on both hygiene and physical education. One is a fundamental solution, and the other is a temporary solution. Neither can be overemphasized. European women all like to dress up brightly, paint their lips, and cover their faces with powder, thinking that they are doing their best to be beautiful. How can they know that if it is not natural, there is no so-called beauty? Therefore, people with healthy bodies often have blood on their faces. Otherwise, it becomes false beauty rather than true beauty.

▲ Wearing Mourning on Fingers Europeans wear black gauze around their arms to express their sorrow, which is like wearing plain clothes and mourning in our country. It is common to see unhygienic people who do not trim their nails, and dirt accumulates, gradually forming black circles. Europeans call this wearing mourning on their fingers. We must pay attention to this.

▲ At a Loss for Words London, the capital of England, has a humid climate. Except for April, May, June and July, it rains all year round. Dense fog pervades, and sometimes you can't see your fingers when you hold out your hand. We feel lost. If we are physically weak, we will definitely get sick.

▲ Relying on Heaven Our country does not pay attention to hygiene, and it has gradually become a habit. Fortunately, our natural environment is superior to Europe. The climate is mild, the products are abundant, and the sunlight kills germs. As the saying goes, "Relying on heaven for food" is true. We should strive for scientific construction in order to create a perfect China.

▲ Labor is Sacred Our people are known to the world for their hard work and frugality. The opening of the Panama Canal, the Chinese laborers in the European War, and the reclamation of Africa have given great benefits to the people of the world and created international glory. We should build on our inherent virtues, develop them and enhance them.

洞仙歌 177

— Written by Tianxu Wosheng

Mr. Pan Jimeng from Xiashi sent a letter inquiring about the seven Southern Wild lyrics by Shen Taimou, compiled by Mr. Hu Puan in the Southern Society Anthology. The first five were "Dong Xian Ge," which was similar to Xu's old work "Silver Chamber Loneliness." The letter asked who the original author was, etc. According to my recollection, Taimou was an old friend of Xu's, and we were in the same society twenty years ago. We often composed and harmonized to this melody as Xu's work for his wife, which was published in the "Zhuo Zuo Lin" of the Wushen year. At that time, Yang Gu Yun and Shen Taimou both had harmonized versions. I don't know how the original work of Xu was mistakenly published as Nan Ya's work in the Southern Society collection. Someone had inquired about this matter in a letter before, seemingly in the fifth collection of the Southern Society ten years ago. At that time, Nan Ya was still alive. Xu then wrote a Ci-hua (poetry talk) in the "Freedom Forum," saying that his disciple Teng Zhixin mistakenly published four "Dong Xian Ge" poems, composed in harmony between Xu and Yi Shifu. He wrongly took Shifu's "Sea Red Curtain Outside" as Xu's original song and Xu's harmonized work as Shifu's harmonization. It was not until the second edition that the error was corrected. Generally, it was due to mistakes in transcription at the time, misreading handwriting. There are many such cases in ancient collections. For example, "The irresistible fall of flowers," and "The familiar returning swallows." Who was the original author remains unproven. This is also a good story in the history of Ci. Therefore, I pick up the old tune to mourn Nan Ya. The poem says: Once parted from the human world, further than Penglai Mountain. Old things should not be mentioned, like a white fan. (Around the founding of the Republic, Taimou wanted to write a legend about a Miss Bai, but Taimou wrote to say that this lady had married, so please stop writing.) The deep red feelings, the green meanings, the willows dark and flowers bright, have all become poems of meeting again in another life. Now, the goddess of Luo River has ascended to heaven, and old Chen Si (Cao Zhi) is aging. A hundred years of fleeting time have passed more than half. Only the white-haired sighs remain, drawing and sewing on paper, yet there is no use for Zhaoyun (a concubine of Su Shi) to accompany. If it weren't for Su Dongpo's understanding of Zen, perhaps through several ups and downs, the heart would break the same way.

Bansong Garden Orchid Appreciation Record 178

— Written by Yinong

I have a lifelong passion for orchids. If a friend cultivates orchids, I always invite myself to appreciate them. On the third day of the Flower Festival, there was an orchid competition at Bansong Garden. I was delighted to hear about it because I had been living in the noisy city of Shanghai, feeling uneasy and restless. I had long wanted to find a secluded place to breathe fresh air. On that day, I went with my friends Li Xueou and Lin Lihu by car. Upon arriving at Bansong Garden, we entered and walked around a winding corridor. Immediately, we smelled a unique fragrance. Upon reaching the hall, it felt like entering a garden of nine acres, clean and dust-free, fragrant and lovely. Graceful and elegant, charming and graceful, orchids were displayed all around, arranged in varying heights. There were more than two hundred pots of orchids. The flower petals had the shapes of lotus petals, plum petals, and crabapple petals. The flower centers had plain centers, red centers, and purple centers. The colors varied: jade, emerald, and light lake green. Famous varieties were scattered everywhere, each with its own unique charm. The leaves swayed gracefully, and the flowers seemed to smile charmingly. I and my friends drank tea among them, appreciating them in silence. I only felt that the fragrance was quiet and solemn, and the teeth and cheeks retained the fragrance. Mr. Li Xueou said, "All flowers have fragrance, but only the fragrance of orchids is rich and clear. All flowers have color, but only the color of orchids is deep green and beautiful. Therefore, in the cliffs and empty valleys, they sprout and take root, not fragrant just because no one is around. Orchids are the fragrance of the nation, and are worthy of treasuring. Among them, the most precious and lovely is a kind with ochre and ink colors, the flower luster is ancient and lush, and the charm is serene and elegant, which is especially admired by me, similar to the Guanyin orchid of Guangdong. I saw it once in the 'Spring Retention' painting by the Old Man Hong Zili. It is also rare among orchid cultivators in Shanghai." I then recalled the dozens of orchids I had cultivated at home, all of which were excellent varieties from Fujian and Guangdong. Over the years, I have been occupied with matters and have not been able to settle down. So I left the orchids to face the wind and snow, without caring for or watering them. Seeing these orchids today, I cannot help but sigh. I also wonder what my beloved orchids at home are like today. Recently, the orchid cultivators in Shanghai have each presented their fine works for competition. Their efforts in cultivation have not been small. I and my friends sat silently, sketching flowers, feeling the fragrance surrounding the brush and ink. Lin Lihu painted them, vividly resembling their shapes. Their tranquility is like that of fairies, their gracefulness is like that of beauties, their purity is like that of high scholars, and their elegance is like that of poets. It is difficult to distinguish the flowers from the paintings at first glance. Isn't this the ultimate skill of the divine craftsmanship? I then composed three quatrains to praise them, which are appended below. The spring breeze is light and unrestrained, with a faint fragrance that is charming. The jade soul and ice spirit have traces of the moon. The quality of the flowers should be pure and elegant, and the worldly dust should not be allowed to reach this famous garden. A branch of unique and extraordinary flowers sprouts. I have long admired the "Spring Retention" painting. Now, I meet the fragrant tracks in person, revealing the flower luster that is unparalleled in the world. How is the scenery of my hometown recently? I dream of the sparse shadows of flowers in the courtyard. For ten years, I have written complaints in vain, longing to build a hut with a cloud-covered hoe.

Eulogy for Xu Yusun 179

— Written by Xishen

Mr. Xu was gentle and refined. He worked at the "Xinwenbao" for more than ten years. His friends and colleagues all loved and respected him. One evening this spring, on his way home from the newspaper office, he was ambushed by thugs. Everyone who heard of it felt grief and regret.

Xu Ruzi is an elite of our party, refined and gentle. He unexpectedly died in a ditch. How inhuman are the bandits!

Who was it that robbed and killed Lord Lai Shu? Murderous intent is rampant. Is it only the road to Shu that is difficult? Is the root of all evil society?

Eulogy for Mr. Liu Lianfang of Jingjiang 180

— Written by Xishen

Mr. Lianfang was from a prominent family in Jingjiang. His respected father was a Jinshi (successful candidate in the highest imperial examinations) and served as the magistrate of important counties. Lianfang presided over local public affairs and founded the Jicheng Daily and various industries. He had the style of Zhang Nantong (Zhang Jian). Public opinion was unanimous. He excelled at poetry and prose, and his calligraphy in the regular script style captured the essence of Li Bei Hai (Li Yong). In the late Qing Dynasty, I was the English lecturer at the Jingjiang School. We often visited each other. Recently, Lianfang was in charge of compiling the Jingjiang County Annals. Before his talent could be fully realized, he suddenly passed away. I was shocked to hear the news and wrote a couplet to mourn him.

Recalling past travels like geese alighting on snow, small gatherings with zithers and wine, I was honored to be a guest in Li Bei Hai's presence.

A prominent figure was promoted in Ji Sha, greatly promoting the atmosphere, and was a person who could be written about in Nantong's biography.

The Ancestor of Tobacco 181

— Written by Qiulang

Recently, when friends and relatives meet, in addition to offering tea, they often add cigarettes to show respect. However, according to the old customs of our country, there was originally no tobacco. It was not until the late Ming Dynasty that snuff appeared. This is based on Zhao Zhiqian's "Yonglu Leisure Talk," which states, "Snuff comes from Italy in the Atlantic Ocean. In the ninth year of the Wanli reign of the Ming Dynasty, Matteo Ricci sailed into Guangdong and introduced it to China." From this, it is known that snuff was indeed the ancestor of tobacco. It is inhaled through the nose, not held in the mouth. Later, Chinese people researched tobacco materials and made their own water pipes, hand-rolled cigarettes, and other types, each according to their preferences. In recent years, cigarettes have become popular, and the former is almost eliminated, while those who use snuff are even rarer than morning stars. However, snuff was quite popular among high-ranking officials and monks at the time. However, the price was surprisingly high. The best quality cost about fifty taels of gold per tael. It is said that Ouyang Lin, a former official of Jiangxi Province, had a particular addiction to it. Every year, he spent four to five thousand taels of gold on it and had a large collection of snuff bottles, all of which were treasures. He often fondled them for pleasure during his leisure time.

Stray Jade Studio's American Tour Notes 182

— Written by Lai

The recent situation is excellent. It is still very crowded every day. Yesterday (Friday), the audience was especially enthusiastic. When "Fen He Wan" was finished, the curtain call was requested as many as seven times because the audience could truly understand it. Those who have heard it spread the word more and more widely. The more people who come to listen, the more they enjoy it. At present, the audience laughs at all the humorous and funny parts of the play, which proves that they can quite understand it.

The entire faculty of Columbia University held a tea party, specially inviting Wanhua (Mei Lanfang) to attend. More than two hundred people attended. The president's wife gave a special reception. Wan gave a speech, saying that he was very honored to be here today, but the purpose of his trip was to study in the United States, like a student. He hoped that all the professors would treat him as a student and not be stingy with their teachings. As for this performance, he was very grateful for the praise and support of the gentlemen, which resulted in a successful outcome. He hoped to receive more guidance in the future, etc. The guests and hosts dispersed happily.

Also, the International Student Association held a public banquet for Wanhua the day before yesterday and invited him to give a speech. More than one thousand people attended. Wan gave an impromptu speech, saying that he had long heard that the United States had established this association, which allowed students of different nationalities to gather together and connect the feelings of various countries. The intention was very good. Lanfang was very happy to be able to come here. This time, he came to the United States to study drama, and his qualifications were the same as those of students. He also wanted to absorb Western civilization and contribute to his motherland. He hoped to receive guidance from time to time.

Currently, small cities in the South have invited him to perform, but each place is mostly short-term, and the procedures for arranging luggage and transportation are complicated and expensive. Therefore, it is planned to perform in New York for five weeks and then rest for ten days in order to travel and visit various theater organizations. Then, he will perform in Chicago for six or seven days and then go to San Francisco. He will stay there for more than a month. (March 6)

Warmth in the Heart (172) 183

— Written by Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 10: Crimson Flames Rise to the Sky, Girl Filially Serves as an Actress; Red Carpet on the Floor, Meeting Famous Actors on the Spot.

The fire fighting in Shanghai is considered quite rapid. In a short while, the fire weakened. Zuo Shichen smiled and said, "Just now, you heard the noisy sounds downstairs. Some people were arguing about a name called Ah Huo. Who knew that it wasn't Ah Huo arguing, but a real fire coming. Didn't I say that water could overcome fire? Now, watering with the water in the leather belt immediately extinguished it. It was all proven in a short while." While watching the fire gradually recede, everyone was a little relieved when a elder sister from the Zhu Feng family across the room, named Ah Bao, ran upstairs, saying, "It's very dangerous! It's very dangerous! Someone almost burned to death!" Hearing this, everyone gathered around to ask, "Sister Ah Bao, who are you talking about?" Ah Bao said, "It's the family where the fire started!" At this time, Ruiyun asked anxiously, "How did the fire start?" Ah Bao said, "I heard them say that the fire started from catching bedbugs. Isn't the family in that alley the family of Gonggong Da Wang Wen Guizhi?" The eldest aunt said, "It's not just the Wen Guizhi family. There are a total of four families in their three-story house." Ah Jin said, "Eldest aunt, don't interrupt her. Let her continue to talk about how the fire started." Ah Bao said, "I also know that there are four families in this alley, but the fire started in the Wen Guizhi family. Wen Guizhi's good mother (grandmother) is a bit hemiplegic. They don't have a small room. Everyone lives in the business area. Wen Guizhi's good mother is not in good health and went to bed early. She woke up at eleven o'clock after being bitten by bedbugs. She got up to catch bedbugs. She slept in the toilet room behind them. They do business, and there is no electric light installed in the toilet room. There was an oil lamp on the table. The old lady fell asleep for a while and felt itchy in her neck. Knowing that it was because of bedbugs, she struck a match and lit the oil lamp to catch bedbugs. When she turned over the pillow, there were indeed several large bedbugs. The old lady's hand was already trembling a little. Seeing the bedbugs, she was anxious to catch them, but she knocked over the oil lamp. You can imagine how powerful kerosene is. It catches fire when it sees fire. The old lady, who is Wen Guizhi's grandmother, saw that the mosquito net was already on fire and quickly tore it down, but other places were also on fire. The old lady was so panicked that she had to shout for help. She splashed water from the washbasin on it, but it wouldn't go out. In a while, the pillow and quilt were all on fire. No matter how hard she tried to extinguish it, she couldn't put it out. The eldest aunt said, "That old lady must have been frightened. Otherwise, she could have just covered it with the quilt and put it out. Cover it with the quilt and don't let it get air. This is a good way. Once, we had a fire in the countryside, and we put it out using this method."

Business News

Financial Gold Standard Suddenly Turns Downward 184

▲ Swap quotes show short sellers offering around two taels

Yesterday, the gold market was generally stable, with daily fluctuations of about three taels. However, interbank trading was not very active. Because the swap market has already reached June, the exchange opened at 8:30 in the morning. The initial swap quote was only 1 tael and 3 or 4 qian, then increased to 2 taels and 1 or 2 qian, and at noon it was 2 taels, all offered by short sellers to long buyers. Because the long side was unwilling to lightly sell off, it was higher than the previous month. As for the May strips, there were no transactions. Most were changed to June as the main month. The opening price in the morning was 502 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen. The closing price at noon was 502 taels and 2 qian, an increase of 4 qian compared to the day before yesterday. This was based on the June price, and the listing was changed. As usual, the suspended listing was cancelled for the after-market.

▲ June gold standard has already entered the market

Yucheng Yong and Yuansheng, among others, have made purchases for June, while Wanxing and Jin'an have sold. The market seemed slightly firmer after the large morning volume decreased slightly. Later, sellers dominated, and the market softened and weakened, fluctuating around 500 taels. There was no significant improvement or deterioration in exchange rates. Later in the market, Fuchang advanced slightly, and Shunli and Yuanxing Yong sold some. However, the foreign exchange market was particularly quiet because it was Wednesday, when there is usually no formal market. Afterwards, the market suddenly became sluggish, and sellers became active, causing the market to decline sharply. It unexpectedly broke below 499 taels from above 500 taels. The psychology of traders turned sparse.

▲ Noon closing still outside the 500 tael mark

Yesterday, the recent British silver bar remained unchanged, and the forward price decreased by one-sixteenth. The silver price also decreased by one-fourth. The opening price for the June gold standard was 500 taels and 3 qian. Then, there were fluctuations of more than one tael. Transactions within the market moved in and out rapidly. The gross price fell from 501 taels and 1 qian to 499 taels and a half. Because the exchange rate remained stable, the June British gold bank paid 11 pence 3125 when the initial price was announced, so the price was 500 taels 8 qian 9 fen. The price did not change. The internal price seemed firm. China Bank sold 1.04625 taels of June gold, and soon after, Mitsui sold 1.0425 taels of July. East Asia offered forward British gold at 11 pence 3125. There were still many sellers on the table, and the price immediately depreciated by two taels. After 10:30, the price was 500 taels. After 11:00, the market was quite flat. Then, Yucheng Yong and others bought in. Maijia Li absorbed the forward British gold at 11 pence 3125, so it was slightly better by 3 or 4 qian. At 11:45, the price was 500 taels and 4 qian. Soon after, it dropped slightly. However, the foreign exchange rate stabilized, and transactions were very rare. At the noon closing, the price was 500 taels and 2 qian, and the announced price was still 508 taels and 8 qian, a decrease of more than 8 taels.

▲ Afternoon market suddenly declines, sharply falling by two taels

The afternoon market opened at 500 taels and 2 qian. Soon after, Indian exchange rates were reported high, and Yuanxing Yong and others hurriedly unloaded their holdings. However, because it was Wednesday, various exchange rates lacked a market. At 4:15, it suddenly fell to 98 taels and 3 qian. By 4:30, it had recovered to 98 taels and 7 qian at the closing. The highest price for the day was 501 taels and 1 qian, and the lowest price was 498 taels and 3 qian, a fluctuation of 2 taels and 8 qian. The announced price decreased by 10 taels. The account for the next month was the same at 502 taels for June and 500 taels for the previous month. The water supplement was 502 taels in the morning, and the water supplement was 1 tael. Transactions in the market have gradually become prosperous, leading to a gradual increase in the lishi price. Although the trend is not rapid, it is easy to increase by several lishi day by day. The use of silver funds is gradually increasing, but it is not very liquid, so the situation has not been fully developed. It is difficult to expect a high rise in silver discounts for a while, but with frequent transfers, a turnaround is expected soon.

Banks to Close Tomorrow 189

Tomorrow (the 18th), which is Friday, is Qingming festival, all foreign businesses and banks on the Bund will be closed for three days according to the precedent, with one day to be supplemented on Sunday. Banks will be closed for four days: the 18th, 19th, 20th and 21st. For the Chinese banks, such as the Central, China, Transportation and Communications Bank and other commercial banks, they are the same as the foreign banks, and will be closed for four days. Other Chinese banks, like the Hong Kong National, Agricultural and Industrial Bank, and Xinhua Bank, will be closed for about two days. In addition, small banks will be closed for one day, and Sunday afternoon will be closed for half a day as usual.

Yarn and Cotton 192

Yarn Market Advances Steadily 193

The yarn market is stable and the situation is relatively firm. Buyers are taking a strong stance. Due to the approaching delivery dates, speculators without goods have to cover their short positions. Therefore, despite the sharp declines in overseas yarn prices, the local market has not been drawn into the vortex. Most speculators in the market have a bearish outlook due to the unstable political situation and busy agricultural season. However, some manufacturers are secretly acting to reduce stocks of yarn in warehouses. Therefore, it is feared that yarn prices will not fall sharply this month, and the future is uncertain.

▲Man-made Fiber Slightly Rises by Half a Taels. At the opening of the man-made fiber market, sentiment was weak due to the sharp fall in US cotton prices. Most people expected a decline of 700-800 cash. However, after the opening, the near-month bulls held firm, and selling was not strong, with a decline of only 100-200 cash. The situation in the second and third sessions tightened sharply, and prices rose in all months. As a result, near-month contracts rose by 100 cash, while far-month contracts fell by 200 cash. In the afternoon, the market sentiment for man-made fiber became even stronger. It was reported that actual sales were good, and speculators covered their short positions, resulting in increases of 200, 300, 400, and 500 cash. The price of third-grade yarn fell particularly sharply. According to the daily trading statistics, 9,600 bales were traded. The closing prices of man-made fiber are listed below:

Grains: Rice Market Suddenly Rises by 200 Cash 196

▲Zhabei: Yesterday, few merchants arrived, and accumulated stocks were becoming scarce due to active sales. Demand for Northern Japonica rice was particularly strong. Retail shops were very eager to buy. Merchants gradually began to sell at higher prices because the supply from inland areas was dwindling and production prices were firm. Recently, rice boats traveling from inland areas to Shanghai were sometimes detained en route due to misunderstandings. Some boatmen changed their plans and sold their rice along the way. At the same time, some boats stopped transporting rice due to banditry. As a result, the supply of rice arriving in Shanghai has been very limited lately. Therefore, the previously sluggish Japonica rice market has suddenly risen by 200 cash. The supply of Bo-dao rice is also scarce, and prices are improving. Yangxian rice has also risen sharply, and buyers are actively searching for it, with prices rising by about 200 cash. Du-ke-bu and other types of Xian rice are still sluggish. Although the market was initially uninspired, it has now strengthened along with other commodities. High-quality rice is opening at around 18 yuan.

▲Hu-nan: The rice market was initially stable but tightened later. Buying interest in the morning market was moderate. However, the market improved after news of price increases from the north. The arrival of rice from the river areas was very limited. Changshu and Wuxi Japonica rice prices increased due to active sales. Su-tong-ji Japonica rice sales in the street were moderate. Large-scale transactions were high, but smaller ones were stable. The sales of Qingjiao and Xi-yong Bo-dao rice from the south were slightly brisk. Arrivals were limited, and prices rose by about 100 cash. Early rice sales were also brisk. The high-quality rice mentioned above opened at around 18 yuan. Yangxian rice stocks were dwindling, and supplies were not smooth. Market sentiment shifted from stable to firm and expensive. Customer merchants and rural sales were paying close attention. Furthermore, with the price of foreign rice rising steadily, domestic Xian rice felt particularly desirable. Prices rose by 150 cash. Shadow market transactions were slightly better, with buyers carefully selecting high-quality rice, reaching a market price of 16.90 yuan.

Futures Foreign Rice Continues to Rise 197

Yesterday, the foreign rice market conditions were even better. Sales to Nanjing, Changshu, Wuxi, and Kunshan were particularly strong, sales to Hangzhou were slightly lighter, and sales to Ningbo and Shaoxing were intermittent. Sales in this street were also good. 10,000 bags of spot rice were opened. Foreign rice futures firms shouted higher prices and were unwilling to sell much because people's hearts were getting better and better. Returned rice was increasingly firm. Flour Market Near-Term Flat, Distant-Term Weak 198

Yesterday, the flour market was generally flat and weak. The near-term contract reached a low of 2.5375 taels this month, but then recovered slightly as speculators covered their short positions, even though actual sales were not good. As for the distant-term contracts, the outlook for the various months was bright due to the clear weather and warmer climate. General inland bulls were hesitant to take further positions, as the relationship between sunny and rainy weather and the annual wheat harvest seemed to be a widespread consideration. However, although distant-term market values were high, manufacturers' sales were still not smooth. In addition, the peak price of rice repeatedly reached new highs, making it difficult for all inland merchants to overcome at once. As a result, the near-term contract was up 2.5 cash from the previous day, May down 2.5 cash, June down 7.5 cash, July down 10 cash, August down 7.5 cash, and September down 5 cash, it is said.

Green and Yellow Wheat Market Softens 199

Yesterday, wheat futures uniformly softened. Problems had arisen with settlement for the near-term contract, and there was no longer any intention to continue delivery for this month. Although the arrival of high-quality goods from various sources in recent days was not large, inventories were gradually increasing. Therefore, people's hearts were weakened, and many people were selling. This phenomenon during the green and yellow season was good news for a portion of the people's diet. The outlook for distant-term contracts in the various months had changed due to the clear weather, and previous concerns about rain had now changed their outlook. Furthermore, prices for new goods arriving at this price were so high that they could not go any higher, as they were too close to the price of old goods, making them too risky. Therefore, sellers in the various months became more active, and the market gradually fell. As a result, April and June contracts were down 30 cash from the previous day, July down 20 cash, and August and September contracts each down 30 cash. As for spot wheat, only Fuxin was still able to continue purchasing due to the current factory appetite. Most others were watching due to weak flour sales. Therefore, the prices of various grades fell sharply, differing by 100 cash from the highest prices of the previous week. Wheat from Qingjiangpu and Suzhou opened at 5.1 taels and 5.07 taels, Shaoxing wheat at 5.06 taels, and Anqing and Jiangxi wheat at 5.02 taels, 5.0 taels, 4.8 taels, and 4.6 taels, for a total of 9,000 bags, which were purchased by factories such as Fuxin, it is said.

Recent News on New Tea from Wu and Qi 200

▲Wu-yi: The tea bushes in Zhouyuan have shown green buds in the last ten days due to continuous spring rains and warm weather. After yesterday becoming extremely hot, both old and new tea bushes were showing green tips. The early ones were growing like sparrow tongues. Tea that was fertilized, loosened, weeded, etc., was especially lush and green. Mountain tea and tea that had been damaged by snow last winter had not yet sprouted. Yesterday (the 7th), a sudden wind and hail storm struck, and many of the tea buds that had sprouted were knocked off. According to tea farmers, the tea leaves were damaged by this storm, and the harvest would have to be reduced by another tenth.

▲Qi-fu: Recently, the development of black tea has been rapid due to the warm weather and intermittent rain and sunshine. The earliest tea leaves can be harvested in the middle of the month. Tea masters and workers from various firms are heading into the mountains to prepare for the opening of the season. However, due to the lack of current cash in Jingzhen and Tunxi, most firms have not yet received all of their funds. In addition, tea houses have tightened their foreign exchange lending. This year, only Zhongxin and Chunshen firms are going into the mountains to receive customers and issue tickets. The remaining firms are still watching. Therefore, the originally planned continuation of tea houses in Fudi has been temporarily suspended due to the impact of the tight money supply. Overall, the number of tea houses in Fudi has been reduced by five-tenths compared to the old days, and the market appears to be in a downturn.

It is heard that foreign companies in Shanghai have no intention of lowering prices for 25.7-25.8 taels, and their desire for lower prices seems to be stronger than that of Hankou. However, due to the high prices in Zhejiang, it is not easy to fall too much. Therefore, it has not been allowed to approach for a while. Yesterday, according to the Hankou telegram, foreign companies bought 400-500 tons, priced at 25 taels in foreign regulations. According to the source, the stock has been rising strongly, with an estimated tens of thousands of dan. Customer demand has not yet been opened. In addition, there are tens of thousands of dan of Xiangtung that are already on the way and will arrive soon. If this batch arrives, if the foreign market does not trade, the market may have to fall further, it is also not known.

Business News 204

▲China Yapu Ear Electrical Appliance Factory Co., Ltd. announced that the company held a general meeting of shareholders yesterday at the Central Sichaifu Restaurant. Shareholders Wang Boyuan, Zhao Zhongying, Qin Runqing, Hu Xiyuan, Wu Songsheng, and others with over 2,000 shares attended. Zhou Baoguang was publicly elected as chairman, and the ceremony was performed as usual. General Manager Hu Xiyuan reported on the business situation of the 18th year and discussed expanding the business. In addition to the original light bulbs, electric fans, electric stoves, and electrical products were added. Then, the directors and supervisors were re-elected. As a result, Qin Runqing, Wang Boyuan, Zhang Zuying, Zhao Shenying, He Gusheng, Zhou Baoguang, and Hu Zu'an were elected as directors, and He Peiyuan, Liang Chenlan, and Wang Fengnian were elected as supervisors. Hu Xiyuan continued to serve as general manager, Liang Zuguang as associate manager, and Sun Xiangpu as factory director. After the meeting, a meal was served, and it was already nine o'clock when the meeting dispersed, it is said.

▲Xu Family Three Hundred and Three Soda Water Factory announced that the factory is operated by German merchants, and the staff they hired have extensive experience in soda water. The technician, "Saninas", SANIFAS, was previously hired by a large soda water factory in Shanghai with a large salary, but he did not take office. Now he is dedicating all his efforts to the factory. It is expected that after the products are launched, they will be able to lead the soda water industry. Sample water will be available soon, it is said.

▲Flying Step Leather Shoe Company announced that it recently established a public store at No. 38 Jiangxi Road, near the intersection of Nanjing Road, which has now opened. The Chinese manager is Mr. Shen Tingzhang, who previously worked in the leather shoe department of Welfare Company. The company's leather shoes have novel styles and solid quality, no different from imported goods. Everything is supervised and manufactured in Shanghai by famous German craftsmen, so the prices are very low, and the quality is the best, it is said.

▲New World Hotel on Tibet Road announced that since the opening of the hotel, the business has been thriving. The clean interior rooms have long been praised by guests from all walks of life. It is now planned to add a bookstore. Renowned storytellers and ballad singers are being hired and arrangements are being made, and it will be realized soon.

▲Far East Stamp Company announced that the company specializes in selling world stamps at cost-effective prices, and also sells various match labels, postal cards, and other interesting items. Recently, the Japanese government held a completion commemoration meeting for the imperial capital reconstruction project. The post office specially made a special postmark to stamp commemorative mail. The company has already shipped many postcards with special postmarks and sells them at low prices. A business catalog is available. Send a letter with postage and it will be sent immediately. The company is located at No. 31 Tiancheng Lane, Jaxi Road, French Concession, it is said.

Group News 205

▲Business Consolidation Association announced that the commercial library of the association has been open for a long time and has a collection of Chinese and Western books, magazines, and newspapers, with over 50,000 copies. The original location was not large enough, and some of the books were placed on the gatehouse, making it inconvenient to borrow. The director of the library yesterday discussed with the executive committee to move the reading room to the side of the conference hall, and the original location was used as a library room, changing the entrance and exit and the borrowing room. Work has begun and is being completed day and night, and it can be completed in a week.

▲Dog Breeding Association announced that the dog show to be held by the association has been scheduled to begin on May 17 (Saturday) at the Racecourse. The number of applicants this time is very enthusiastic, and the competition rules have been expanded, such as the preliminary competition and the Chinese breed competition, which are the most interesting. The preliminary competition is for dogs that have never won first prize. The Chinese breed competition is for all dogs born in China. Those who wish to join the competition are requested to obtain the rules from Mr. Ge Lin of Eagle Steel Plant, No. 8 Museum Road, as soon as possible. There are not many registration dates left, and registration will be closed on May 3. Mrs. Smith has donated two silver shields, specially given to the best male and female dogs bred by Chinese people in the exhibition, it is said.

▲Shang Wu Jin De Association, initiated by Li Jinglin, Xu Jingren, Zhang Zhaodong, Jiang Rongqiao, etc., announced that the association has been established for many years and has achieved outstanding results. It has compiled 15 kinds of martial arts series, which are published by the World Martial Arts Bookstore. Now, after the general meeting, it has been decided to expand the association's affairs. Han Muxia and Zhang Zhaodong will be in charge of education, and Zhao Daoxin, a famous martial arts expert, will be hired as the chief professor. Martial arts books will continue to be compiled, and 30 kinds will be published this year. The general office is still located on Ganshi East Road, French Concession, it is said.
